局限 / 后续问题: 当前局部NNP架构显著低估了实验溶剂化自由能，表明其无法充分描述离子溶剂化热力学，需要显式长程静电处理来改善。

中文摘要: 镁离子在许多生物过程中发挥着关键作用，但在生物分子模拟中仍然难以准确建模。尽管已付出大量科学努力，经典力场仍无法同时重现关键的结构、热力学和动力学溶液性质，这可能是因为它们无法显式考虑量子多体效应。在此，我们开发并系统基准测试了基于revPBE-D3/zd和revPBE0-D3/zd密度泛函理论参考数据训练的MACE神经网络势（NNPs），用于水合MgCl₂溶液，并评估其重现广泛实验溶液性质的能力，包括第一水合壳结构、扩散系数、活度导数、水交换速率与机制以及溶剂化自由能。两种NNP均准确重现了第一水合壳的八面体结构、离子配对性质和扩散系数。将NNP与过渡路径采样及其他增强采样技术相结合，使我们能够捕捉Mg²⁺第一水合壳中水交换的稀有事件，揭示了解离交换机制。过渡界面采样得到的交换速率在实验值的一个数量级范围内，相比经典解离力场有显著改进。然而，NNP推导的溶剂化自由能显著低估了实验值，揭示了当前局部NNP架构在描述离子溶剂化热力学方面的局限性。我们的结果表明，基于DFT训练的NNP能够准确描述Mg²⁺水合结构、扩散、离子配对和交换动力学，同时突出了需要显式长程静电处理以实现与实验离子溶剂化自由能的定量一致性。

英文原始摘要: Magnesium ions play an essential role in many biological processes but remain challenging to model in biomolecular simulations. Despite considerable scientific effort, classical force fields fail to simultaneously reproduce key structural, thermodynamic and kinetic solution properties, likely due to their inability to explicitly account for quantum many-body effects. Here, we develop and systematically benchmark MACE neural network potentials (NNPs) for aqueous MgCl$_2$ solutions trained on revPBE-D3/zd and revPBE0-D3/zd density functional theory reference data and assess their ability to reproduce a broad range of experimental solution properties including the structure of the first hydration shell, diffusion coefficient, activity derivative, water-exchange rate and mechanism as well as solvation free energy. Both NNPs accurately reproduce the octahedral structure of the first hydration shell, ion pairing properties and diffusion coefficients. Combining the NNPs with transition path sampling and other enhanced sampling techniques allows us to capture the rare event of water exchange in the first hydration shell of Mg$^{2+}$ revealing a dissociative exchange mechanism. Transition interface sampling yields exchange rates within one order of magnitude of experiment, representing a substantial improvement over classical dissociative force fields. In contrast, the NNP-derived solvation free energy significantly underestimates the experimental value, revealing a limitation of the present local NNP architectures for describing ion solvation thermodynamics. Our results demonstrate that DFT-trained NNPs can accurately describe Mg$^{2+}$ hydration structure, diffusion, ion pairing, and exchange kinetics, while highlighting the need for explicit long-range electrostatic treatments to achieve quantitative agreement with experimental ion solvation free energies.

*Zihan Yu,Xianling Zeng,Zhiming Xue,Yalun Qi,Sichen Zhao*

一句话结论: 提出面向AI负载突发的容量压力预警框架，基于XGBoost实现高召回率预测并支持数据中心主动运维干预。

研究问题: 超大规模数据中心中AI工作负载的突发性、高强度和快速变化的资源需求导致突发容量压力，现有基于反应式阈值的机制无法有效应对，缺乏在系统性能下降前进行主动干预的预测能力。

主要创新点: 提出面向部署的、感知突发的早期预警框架，将容量压力预测建模为多变量遥测窗口上的高召回率预测任务，并引入AI负载激增注入方法用于真实条件下的系统评估。


<details>
  <summary>更多信息</summary>

研究动机: AI工作负载（尤其是LLM训练与推理）快速增长，其突发性和高强度特征使传统反应式阈值机制失效，亟需能在系统降级前触发运维干预的主动预测能力。

主要方法: 整合负载强度、时间变化和系统压力信号，采用轻量级XGBoost树模型捕捉高度不平衡环境中的非线性交互，进行高召回率预测；引入AI负载激增注入方法模拟真实突发需求模式；设计面向部署的阈值选择策略。

实验 / 验证: 使用AI负载激增注入方法在真实条件下评估系统，与基线方法进行对比，并采用面向部署的阈值选择策略评估实际检测能力。

主要结果: XGBoost模型实现ROC AUC 0.697、AP 0.670，显著优于基线；在面向部署的阈值选择下召回率达0.914，可检测大多数压力时段且误报成本可接受。

结论: 基于学习的高召回率早期预警系统在AI驱动负载时代具有显著实用价值，可集成到运维控制回路中支持负载限流和资源扩缩容等主动操作，实现弹性和自适应的数据中心运维。

局限 / 后续问题: 

中文摘要: 大规模AI工作负载（尤其是大语言模型训练与推理）的快速增长，正在从根本上重塑超大规模数据中心的运行动态。与传统云工作负载不同，AI驱动的任务表现出突发性、高强度和快速变化的资源需求特征，常导致突发容量压力，而基于反应式阈值机制的策略无法有效应对。本文提出一个面向部署的、感知突发的早期预警框架，用于在AI负载激增下进行主动容量压力预测。我们将该问题建模为多变量遥测窗口上的高召回率预测任务，明确目标是在系统性能下降之前实现运维干预。所提框架整合了负载强度、时间变化和系统压力信号，并采用轻量级基于树的学习模型来捕捉高度不平衡环境中的非线性交互。为在真实条件下评估系统，我们引入了AI负载激增注入方法，模拟大规模AI系统中观察到的突发驱动需求模式。基于XGBoost的模型实现了0.697的ROC AUC和0.670的AP，显著优于基线方法。在面向部署的阈值选择下，该框架实现了0.914的召回率，能够检测到大多数易产生压力的时段，且误报成本可接受。除预测性能外，我们还展示了如何将所提框架集成到运维控制回路中，以支持负载限流和资源扩缩容等主动操作。我们的结果突出了基于学习的高召回率早期预警系统在AI驱动负载时代实现弹性和自适应数据中心运维中的实用价值。

英文原始摘要: The rapid growth of large-scale AI workloads, particularly Large Language Model (LLM) training and inference, is fundamentally reshaping the operational dynamics of hyperscale data centers. Unlike traditional cloud workloads, AI-driven jobs exhibit bursty, high-intensity, and rapidly shifting resource demands, often leading to sudden capacity stress that cannot be effectively handled by reactive threshold-based mechanisms. In this paper, we propose a deployment-oriented, burst-aware early warning framework for proactive capacity stress prediction under AI workload surges. We formulate the problem as a high-recall forecasting task over multivariate telemetry windows, with the explicit goal of enabling operational intervention before system degradation occurs. The proposed framework integrates workload intensity, temporal variation, and system pressure signals, and employs a lightweight tree-based learning model to capture nonlinear interactions in highly imbalanced environments. To evaluate the system under realistic conditions, we introduce an AI workload surge injection methodology that simulates burst-driven demand patterns observed in large-scale AI systems. Our XGBoost-based model achieves an ROC AUC of 0.697 and an AP of 0.670, significantly outperforming baseline methods. Under deployment-oriented threshold selection, the framework achieves a Recall of 0.914, enabling the detection of the majority of stress-prone periods with acceptable false-alarm cost. Beyond predictive performance, we show how the proposed framework can be integrated into operational control loops to support proactive actions such as workload throttling and resource scaling. Our results highlight the practical value of high-recall, learning-based early warning systems in enabling resilient and adaptive data center operations in the era of AI-driven workloads.

### [105] [A Survey on Federated Causal Discovery and Inference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23741v1)
*Xianjie Guo,Yuwei Wang,Guodu Xiang,Xiaoli Tang,Kui Yu,Han Yu,Qiang Yang*

一句话结论: 首个将联邦因果发现与推断统一为互补流程的系统性综述，提供多维度分类体系。

研究问题: 联邦因果发现（FCD）与联邦因果推断（FCI）领域缺乏综合性综述，且该领域跨学科特性导致研究者入门门槛高；此外，以往工作将FCD和FCI割裂处理，未建立二者之间的统一联系。

主要创新点: 首次将FCD和FCI形式化为统一联邦因果推理流程中互补的两个阶段，并基于三个核心设计决策（结构学习方式、数据划分方式、各方获得的结构知识）提出多维度分类体系，涵盖方法论范式、联邦拓扑和结构范围三个轴。


<details>
  <summary>更多信息</summary>

研究动机: 可靠因果分析的数据通常分散在各机构且因隐私法规或通信限制无法集中；联邦学习可在不共享原始数据的前提下实现协作分析，催生了FCD和FCI领域，但该领域跨学科特性强且缺乏系统综述，阻碍了研究者进入。

主要方法: 系统性综述方法。对FCD沿方法论范式、联邦拓扑和结构范围三个轴进行分类组织，并考察时间动态性、数据异构性、缺失数据和非相同变量集等实践维度；对FCI按目标估计量（平均效应vs个体化/条件效应）和估计策略（经典加权到深度生成架构）分类；将FCD与FCI统一为互补流程。

实验 / 验证: 本文为综述性论文，未涉及具体实验，而是对现有文献进行系统性梳理和分类。

主要结果: 构建了FCD和FCI的多维度分类体系，形式化了二者作为统一流程互补阶段的联系，并梳理了隐私、通信效率、理论保证和应用领域等共同关注点。

结论: FCD和FCI应被视为统一联邦因果推理流程中互补的两个阶段，FCD为FCI提供有效效应估计所需的结构知识；未来研究需在隐私保护、通信效率、理论保证和应用拓展等方面解决开放性挑战。

局限 / 后续问题: 综述本身受限于现有文献的覆盖范围；摘要中提到的开放性挑战包括隐私、通信效率、理论保证和应用领域等方面仍待深入研究。

中文摘要: 因果推理涵盖因果结构发现和因果效应推断，是数据驱动决策的基础。在实践中，用于可靠因果分析的数据通常分布在各机构之间，由于隐私法规或通信限制而无法集中。联邦学习（FL）通过在不共享原始数据的情况下实现协作分析来解决这一问题，从而催生了快速发展的联邦因果发现（FCD）与联邦因果推断（FCI）领域。然而，该领域的跨学科特性以及缺乏综合性综述给研究者带来了入门障碍。本文通过提供基于多维度分类的系统综述来弥合这一差距。基于任何FCD解决方案背后的三个核心设计决策——即结构如何被学习、数据如何被划分、以及各方获得何种结构知识——我们从方法论范式、联邦拓扑和结构范围三个轴对FCD进行组织。我们进一步考察了关键的实践维度，包括时间动态性、数据异构性、缺失数据和非相同变量集。对于FCI，我们按照目标估计量（平均处理效应与个体化/条件处理效应）和估计策略（从经典加权方法到现代深度生成架构）对方法进行分类。与以往将FCD和FCI分开处理的工作不同，我们将其联系形式化为统一联邦因果推理流程中互补的两个阶段，其中FCD为FCI中有效的效应估计提供所需的结构知识。最后，我们强调了它们在隐私、通信效率、理论保证和应用领域方面的共同关注点，并通过识别未来研究的开放性挑战来总结全文。

英文原始摘要: Causal reasoning, which encompasses the discovery of causal structures and the inference of causal effects, is fundamental to data-driven decision making. In practice, data for reliable causal analysis are often distributed across institutions and cannot be centralized due to privacy regulations or communication constraints. Federated learning (FL) addresses this by enabling collaborative analysis without raw data sharing, giving rise to the rapidly growing field of federated causal discovery (FCD) and inference (FCI). However, the interdisciplinary nature of this field and the absence of a comprehensive survey present barriers to entry for researchers. This paper bridges that gap by providing a systematic review through multi-dimensional taxonomies. Grounded in the three core design decisions underlying any FCD solution, namely how structures are learned, how data are partitioned, and what structural knowledge each party obtains, we organize FCD along three axes: methodological paradigm, federation topology, and structural scope. We further examine key practical dimensions, including temporal dynamics, data heterogeneity, missing data, and non-identical variable sets. For FCI, we categorize methods by target estimand (average versus individualized/conditional treatment effects) and by estimation strategy, from classical weighting methods to modern deep generative architectures. Unlike prior works that treat FCD and FCI separately, we formalize their connection as complementary stages of a unified federated causal reasoning pipeline, where FCD supplies the structural knowledge required for valid effect estimation in FCI. Finally, we highlight their shared concerns regarding privacy, communication efficiency, theoretical guarantees, and application domains, and conclude by identifying open challenges for future research.

### [106] [Direct stress imaging from shear wave propagation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.25385v1)
*Yiwei Duan,Michel Destrade,Wenchang Tan,Guo-Yang Li*

主分类: 数值计算与科学计算

来源: arxiv

期刊: 

DOI: 

免费全文: [arXiv abstract](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.25385v1), [arXiv pdf](https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.25385v1), [Google Scholar search](https://scholar.google.com/scholar?q=Direct+stress+imaging+from+shear+wave+propagation++free+full+text+pdf)

一句话结论: 提出声弹性成像框架，利用剪切波传播与物理信息学习实现异质材料应力场的非破坏性高分辨率重建。

研究问题: 异质固体中应力无法直接测量，传统方法依赖本构模型从变形推断应力，缺乏无需本构模型假设和材料参数校准的高分辨率应力场成像方法。

主要创新点: 将应力恢复表述为波动方程的反问题，利用声弹性效应结合基于物理信息学习的全剪切波波形反演，从全场波动测量中直接重建波动方程系数，无需显式本构模型或材料参数校准即可估计应力幅值和主方向。


<details>
  <summary>更多信息</summary>

研究动机: 应力不可直接测量，传统推断方法依赖本构模型，在异质材料中难以实现精确的应力场成像，亟需一种非破坏性、高分辨率且不依赖本构模型的应力场重建方法。

主要方法: 利用声弹性效应（预存应力改变局部波动动力学），将应力恢复建模为波动方程反问题，采用基于物理信息学习的全剪切波波形反演，从全场波动测量中重建波动方程系数，进而估计应力幅值和主方向。

实验 / 验证: 通过数值模拟和超声剪切波弹性成像实验，在异质材料中验证该方法对非均匀应力场的重建能力。

主要结果: 实现了亚波长空间分辨率（< 0.28 λ），在异质材料中精确重建了非均匀应力场。

结论: AEI建立了高分辨率应力成像的通用框架，为复杂材料和生物组织中内部力学状态的非侵入性映射提供了可行途径。

局限 / 后续问题: 

中文摘要: 异质固体中应力场的定量成像仍然具有挑战性，因为应力无法直接测量，通常需要利用本构模型从变形中推断。本文提出了声弹性成像（AEI），一种利用剪切波传播重建应力场的非破坏性框架。AEI利用声弹性效应——即预存应力会改变局部波动动力学——并将应力恢复表述为波动方程的反问题。通过基于物理信息学习的全剪切波波形反演，AEI从全场波动测量中重建波动方程系数，从而在无需显式指定本构模型或校准材料参数的情况下，实现应力幅值和主方向的估计。我们通过数值模拟和超声剪切波弹性成像实验，展示了亚波长空间分辨率（< 0.28 λ）以及在异质材料中对非均匀应力场的精确重建。这些结果建立了一个高分辨率应力成像的通用框架，为复杂材料和生物组织中内部力学状态的非侵入性映射提供了途径。

英文原始摘要: Quantitative imaging of stress fields in heterogeneous solids remains challenging because stress is not directly measurable and is typically inferred from deformation using constitutive models. Here we present Acoustoelastic Imaging (AEI), a non-destructive framework for reconstructing stress fields from shear wave propagation. AEI exploits the acoustoelastic effect, whereby pre-existing stress modifies local wave dynamics, and formulates stress recovery as an inverse problem of the governing wave equations. Using full shear waveform inversion with physics-informed learning, AEI reconstructs wave-equation coefficients from full-field wave measurements, enabling estimation of stress magnitude and principal directions without explicit constitutive model specification or material-parameter calibration. We demonstrate sub-wavelength spatial resolution (< 0.28 λ) and accurate reconstruction of nonuniform stress fields in heterogeneous materials through numerical simulations and ultrasound shear wave elastography experiments. These results establish a general framework for high-resolution stress imaging and provide a route toward non-invasive mapping of internal mechanical states in complex materials and biological tissues.

  <summary>更多信息</summary>

主要结果: 前沿模型与人类之间存在巨大差距，拓扑基础和时空推理任务失败最为显著；在模拟数据上微调轻量级模型可提升真实交通场景性能。

结论: OmniTraffic提供了可控、可扩展的交通推理评测与数据生成管线，仿真生成的监督对交通特定多模态推理具有显著价值。

英文原始摘要: Traffic scene understanding requires models to reason beyond object recognition, including lane topology, multi-view geometry, temporal evolution, and signal-phase semantics. However, existing traffic-oriented multimodal benchmarks largely emphasize passive visual recognition or isolated video understanding, offering limited support for evaluating structure-aware traffic reasoning under controlled conditions. We introduce OmniTraffic, a controllable generation pipeline and benchmark for spatio-temporal traffic reasoning. Built around 12 real-world intersections reconstructed into editable 3D traffic environments and complemented by surveillance footage from two countries, OmniTraffic supports both controlled and natural-condition evaluation. It defines a three-level task hierarchy spanning scene perception, multi-view and temporal reasoning, and decision support. Using structured traffic metadata, OmniTraffic generates synchronized multi-view VQA samples covering vehicle states, lane functions, view--BEV correspondence, temporal dynamics, and signal-phase analysis, resulting in 8M VQA samples and a 3K human-verified test set. Evaluation of eleven frontier MLLMs reveals a large human--model gap, with the most pronounced failures in topology-grounded and spatio-temporal reasoning tasks. Fine-tuning a lightweight MLLM on simulated OmniTraffic data further improves performance on real-world traffic scenes, demonstrating the value of simulation-generated supervision for traffic-specific multimodal reasoning. Beyond a fixed dataset, OmniTraffic provides an extensible pipeline with configurable intersections, camera views, traffic demands, signal phases, visual conditions, and rare events.

### [108] [Aggregation as a Double-Edged Sword: Fear, Allee Effects, and Finite-Time Collapse](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17586v1)

DOI: 

免费全文: [arXiv abstract](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17586v1), [arXiv pdf](https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.17586v1), [Google Scholar search](https://scholar.google.com/scholar?q=Aggregation+as+a+Double-Edged+Sword%3A+Fear%2C+Allee+Effects%2C+and+Finite-Time+Collapse++free+full+text+pdf)

一句话结论: 猎物聚集防御在疾病与Allee效应下反而加速生态系统崩溃。

研究问题: 传统观点认为猎物聚集是有效的反捕食防御策略，但在同时存在疾病传播、捕食者诱导恐惧和Allee效应的种群中，聚集行为如何影响生态系统稳定性缺乏理论认识。

主要创新点: 首次推导出灭绝时间的显式上界，量化行为参数（聚集强度、恐惧强度）与种群参数（Allee阈值）如何共同决定生态崩溃速度；将双重恐惧响应、次线性聚集捕食项与Allee效应整合进统一的易感-感染-捕食者模型。


<details>
  <summary>更多信息</summary>

研究动机: 猎物聚集作为防御行为的生态后果在疾病动力学背景下可能被误解，需要揭示行为防御与疾病动力学及种群脆弱性交互时可能产生的突发生态临界点。

主要方法: 构建包含双重恐惧响应、次线性聚集捕食项和Allee效应的易感-感染-捕食者模型；通过分岔分析和双参数延拓方法进行理论分析。

实验 / 验证: 进行了分岔分析（识别跨临界分岔、鞍结分岔和Hopf分岔）以及恐惧-Allee参数平面的双参数延拓分析，划分稳定共存、振荡共存、捕食者排斥和有限时间灭绝的区域。

主要结果: 聚集增强单调扩大有限时间灭绝区域并缩短灭绝时间上界；较弱聚集支持更丰富的共存动力学景观；有限时间灭绝触发感染猎物与捕食者种群的级联崩溃，最终导致整个生态群落灭绝。

结论: 种群水平的行为防御在与疾病动力学和种群脆弱性相互作用时，可产生突发的生态临界点；聚集防御在特定条件下反而加速而非延缓生态崩溃。

局限 / 后续问题: 

中文摘要: 猎物聚集被广泛认为是抵御捕食的防御策略，然而我们表明，在受捕食者诱导恐惧和种群Allee阈值影响的疾病结构种群中，聚集反而可能加速生态系统崩溃。我们开发并分析了一个包含双重恐惧响应的易感-感染-捕食者模型，同时引入了次线性的基于聚集的捕食项和Allee效应。关键的是，我们推导出了灭绝时间的显式上界，该上界随捕食压力增加或聚集增强而减小，首次量化了行为和种群参数如何共同决定生态崩溃的速度。这一有限时间灭绝随后触发感染猎物和捕食者种群的级联崩溃，导致整个生态群落灭绝。分岔分析揭示了随恐惧强度、聚集强度和Allee阈值变化而出现的跨临界分岔、鞍结分岔和Hopf分岔。双参数延拓进一步确定了恐惧-Allee参数平面中稳定共存、振荡共存、捕食者排斥和有限时间灭绝发生的精确区域，表明更强的聚集单调地扩大了有限时间灭绝区域，而较弱的聚集则支持更丰富的共存动力学景观。这些结果表明，在种群水平上运作的行为防御在与疾病动力学和种群脆弱性相互作用时，可以产生突发的生态临界点。

英文原始摘要: Prey aggregation is widely regarded as a defense against predation, yet we show that in disease-structured populations subject to predator-induced fear and demographic Allee thresholds, aggregation can paradoxically accelerate ecosystem collapse. We develop and analyze a susceptible-infectious-predator model incorporating dual fear responses -- together with a sublinear aggregation-based predation term and an Allee effect. Critically, we derive an explicit upper bound on the extinction time that decreases as predator pressure increases or aggregation strengthens, quantifying for the first time how behavioral and demographic parameters jointly determine the speed of ecological collapse. This finite-time extinction subsequently triggers a cascade collapse of the infected prey and predator populations, driving the entire ecological community to extinction. Bifurcation analysis reveals transcritical, saddle-node, and Hopf bifurcations as fear intensity, aggregation strength, and Allee threshold vary. Two-parameter continuation further identifies the precise regions of the fear--Allee parameter plane in which stable coexistence, oscillatory coexistence, predator exclusion, and finite-time extinction occur, demonstrating that stronger aggregation monotonically enlarges the finite-time extinction region while weaker aggregation supports a richer landscape of coexistence dynamics. These results demonstrate that behavioral defenses operating at the population level can generate abrupt ecological tipping points when they interact with disease dynamics and demographic vulnerability.

主要结果: 所提方法实现了与完整非线性机载模型相当的预测精度，同时相对于已有基线方法大幅降低了计算成本。

局限 / 后续问题: 

中文摘要: 非线性动力学以及多个效应器之间产生的强耦合破坏了传统线性控制分配技术的基本假设。当飞行进入非线性效应主导的区域时，线性分配器由于模型失配加剧而精度降低，进而损害飞行控制系统的性能和鲁棒性。高保真机载模型和黑箱数据驱动方法可以在整个飞行包线内恢复精度，但前者施加了对实时分配而言不可接受的计算负担，后者则牺牲了验证和故障诊断所需的可解释性。本文通过使用非线性动力学稀疏辨识方法，从代表性飞行数据中学习控制效能映射的显式、物理约束解析模型来解决这些局限性。所得映射紧凑、可解释，且具有解析导数，能够在非线性求解器中实现高效计算，同时额外纳入执行器动力学，而无需机载模型。在线自适应机制监测预测残差，并在检测到显著的被控对象变化时刷新模型，在执行器故障和变化的运行条件下提供优雅的重构。该方法在高保真非线性基准飞机上的一系列激进机动中进行评估，实现了与完整非线性机载模型相当的精度，同时相对于已有基线方法大幅降低了计算成本。

英文原始摘要: Nonlinear dynamics and the strong couplings that arise between multiple effectors undermine the assumptions behind conventional, linear control allocation techniques. When flight enters regimes where nonlinear effects dominate, linear allocators exhibit reduced accuracy due to increased model mismatch, which subsequently degrades performance and robustness of the flight control system. High fidelity onboard models and black box data driven approaches can recover accuracy across the flight envelope, but respectively impose computational burdens prohibitive for real time allocation and sacrifice the interpretability required for verification and fault diagnosis. This paper addresses these limitations by learning an explicit, physics constrained analytical model of the control effectiveness mapping from representative flight data using Sparse Identification of Nonlinear Dynamics. The resulting mapping is compact, interpretable, and admits analytical derivatives, enabling efficient computation within nonlinear solvers that additionally incorporate actuator dynamics, without requiring an onboard model. An online adaptation mechanism monitors prediction residuals and refreshes the model when significant plant changes are detected, providing graceful reconfiguration under actuator failures and varying operating conditions. The methodology is evaluated on a high fidelity nonlinear benchmark aircraft across a range of aggressive maneuvers, achieving accuracy comparable to a full nonlinear onboard model while substantially reducing computational cost relative to established baselines.

### [110] [Extended pseudo-spectral physics-informed neural networks for phase-field models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24660v1)
*Callum Marsh,Radek Erban,Andreas Munch*

研究问题: 相场模型中的体自由能密度和界面厚度参数等本构量在实际中很少事先已知，需要从有限的动态观测数据中推断，而现有方法难以同时恢复体化学势和梯度系数。

主要创新点: 提出扩展伪谱物理信息神经网络（ESPINN）框架，能够从瞬态快照数据同时反演恢复体化学势和未知的梯度系数。

  <summary>更多信息</summary>

研究动机: 相场模型的本构量决定图案形成和微观结构演化，但在实际应用中很少事先已知，亟需从有限的动态观测中高效推断这些量。

主要方法: 开发ESPINN框架，结合伪谱方法与物理信息神经网络，利用瞬态快照数据求解相场模型的逆问题，同时恢复体化学势和梯度系数。

实验 / 验证: 在一维Cahn-Hilliard方程上进行数值实验，分别测试无噪声和有噪声条件下的重构精度，并考察快照数量对鲁棒性的影响。

主要结果: 无噪声条件下重构准确且统计稳定，单对快照即可恢复大量本构信息；有噪声时精度优雅下降，增加快照数量可降低方差并提升鲁棒性。

结论: ESPINN是一种数据高效且物理一致的方法，可有效学习相分离连续介质模型中的自由能结构。

局限 / 后续问题: 仅在了一维Cahn-Hilliard方程上验证，未涉及更高维度或更复杂的相场模型；有噪声条件下重构精度有所下降。

中文摘要: 相场模型在相分离的连续介质描述中起着核心作用，其中体自由能密度和界面厚度参数决定了图案形成与微观结构演化。在实际中，这些本构量很少事先已知，必须从有限的动态观测中推断。本文开发了一种扩展伪谱物理信息神经网络（ESPINN）框架，用于从瞬态快照数据中反演识别相场模型。该框架能够同时恢复体化学势和未知的梯度系数。在一维Cahn-Hilliard方程上的数值实验表明，在无噪声条件下实现了准确且统计稳定的重构，甚至仅从单对快照中即可恢复大量本构信息。在存在噪声的情况下，重构精度优雅下降，增加快照数量通过减少运行间的方差来提高鲁棒性。这些结果确立了ESPINN作为一种数据高效且物理一致的方法，用于学习相分离连续介质模型中的自由能结构。

英文原始摘要: Phase-field models play a central role in the continuum description of phase separation, in which the bulk free-energy density and the interfacial thickness parameter determine pattern formation and microstructural evolution. In practice, these constitutive quantities are rarely known a priori and must be inferred from limited dynamical observations. In this work, an extended pseudo-spectral physics-informed neural network (ESPINN) framework is developed for the inverse identification of phase-field models from transient snapshot data. It enables the simultaneous recovery of both the bulk chemical potential and unknown gradient coefficients. Numerical experiments on the one-dimensional Cahn-Hilliard equation demonstrate accurate and statistically stable reconstruction in the noiseless regime, with substantial constitutive information recoverable from even a single snapshot pair. In the presence of noise, reconstruction accuracy degrades gracefully, and increasing the number of snapshots improves robustness by reducing variance across runs. These results establish ESPINN as a data-efficient and physically consistent approach for learning free-energy structure in continuum models of phase separation.

### [111] [Convergence of Gradient Descent for General Neural Network Architectures Beyond the NTK Regime](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23364v1)
*Yuqing Wang*

主分类: 数值计算与科学计算

来源: arxiv

期刊: 

DOI: 

免费全文: [arXiv abstract](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23364v1), [arXiv pdf](https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.23364v1), [Google Scholar search](https://scholar.google.com/scholar?q=Convergence+of+Gradient+Descent+for+General+Neural+Network+Architectures+Beyond+the+NTK+Regime++free+full+text+pdf)

一句话结论: 提出超越NTK的通用架构梯度下降收敛框架，证明在温和条件下GD几乎必然收敛到稳定点邻域。

研究问题: 现有训练动力学理论分析在NTK机制之外难以推广到一般现代神经网络架构，缺乏对多层Transformer等复杂结构的收敛性保证。

主要创新点: 在网络模块层面构建了超越NTK机制的通用收敛框架，通过解析性与零测度论证建立依赖于迭代的PL型不等式，并结合多项式广义光滑性与局部松弛耗散条件证明轨迹上的Lipschitz光滑性。


<details>
  <summary>更多信息</summary>

研究动机: 训练动力学对理解神经网络至关重要，但现有理论难以处理现代通用架构，亟需一个超越NTK机制、适用于预归一化多层Transformer等架构的收敛分析框架。

主要方法: 在网络模块层面建立收敛框架；利用解析性和零测度论证证明依赖于迭代的PL型不等式；通过多项式广义光滑性和局部松弛耗散条件证明GD轨迹上的Lipschitz光滑性；在Xavier初始化和实际架构缩放下解释理论结果。

实验 / 验证: 本文为理论分析工作，未涉及实证实验，但在Xavier初始化和实际架构缩放条件下对定理进行了理论解释。

主要结果: 证明了在温和假设下，对于几乎所有初始化，常规学习率的GD收敛到稳定点邻域；学习率尺度取决于深度和有效瓶颈维度而非最大宽度；推导了残差连接与函数复合的结构非退化含义及全局极小值的通用刻画。

结论: 该框架为NTK机制之外的广泛现代神经网络架构提供了GD收敛性保证，揭示了学习率尺度与架构深度及瓶颈维度的关系，并对残差连接和函数复合的结构性质给出了理论刻画。

局限 / 后续问题: 

中文摘要: 训练动力学是理解神经网络的核心，然而即使对于简单架构，其理论分析仍然困难，对于一般现代架构则更具挑战性。本文提出了一种收敛框架，用于分析在神经正切核（NTK）机制之外的广泛神经网络架构和数据集下的梯度下降（GD）动力学。该框架在网络模块层面构建，涵盖包括预归一化多层Transformer在内的架构。具体而言，在温和假设下，我们证明了对于几乎所有初始化，采用常规学习率的GD收敛到稳定点的邻域。该结论主要通过以下方式证明：利用解析性和零测度论证建立依赖于迭代的PL型不等式，以及通过多项式广义光滑性和局部松弛耗散条件证明GD轨迹上的Lipschitz光滑性。我们进一步在Xavier初始化和实际架构缩放下解释了该定理，表明学习率尺度取决于深度和有效瓶颈维度，而非最大宽度。最后，我们推导了残差连接和函数复合的结构非退化含义，并在我们的框架内提供了全局极小值的通用刻画。

英文原始摘要: Training dynamics is central to understanding neural networks, yet its theoretical analysis remains difficult even for simple architectures and becomes substantially more challenging for general modern architectures. In this paper, we propose a convergence framework for analyzing gradient descent (GD) dynamics under a broad family of neural network architectures and datasets beyond the neural tangent kernel (NTK) regime. The framework is formulated at the level of network blocks and covers architectures including pre-normalized multi-layer transformers. More precisely, under mild assumptions, we prove that for almost all initializations, GD with regular learning rates converges to the neighbourhood of a stationary point. This is mainly proved by establishing an iterate-dependent PL-type inequality through analyticity and measure-zero arguments, and by proving Lipschitz smoothness along the GD trajectory through polynomial generalized smoothness and a local relaxed dissipative condition. We further interpret the theorem under Xavier initialization and practical architectural scaling, showing that the learning rate scale depends on the depth and effective bottleneck dimensions rather than the largest width. Finally, we derive structural nondegeneracy implications for residual connections and function composition, and provide a generic characterization of global minimizers within our framework.

</details>

实验 / 验证: 在调幅分解问题上进行了大量实验，与纯数据驱动基线方法进行对比，评估微观组织形貌再现、统计特征和演化趋势的准确性。

主要结果: 物理引导方法在预测精度、长期稳定性、跨空间分辨率鲁棒性方面均优于纯数据驱动基线，更忠实地再现了微观组织形貌和演化趋势。

结论: 该框架在保持全卷积架构计算效率的同时，通过物理约束弥合了物理模拟与数据驱动代理建模的差距，为数字孪生驱动的微观组织演化预测提供了可靠高效的方案。

局限 / 后续问题: 

中文摘要: 理解和预测微观组织演化是材料设计的核心，然而纯数据驱动的时空学习模型往往存在物理一致性有限和长期预测精度下降的问题。在本工作中，我们提出了一种用于微观组织演化预测的物理引导全卷积时空学习框架。与以往的自监督方法不同，该方法将控制物理方程显式地纳入训练目标，从而促使所学动力学与已知的热力学和动力学定律保持一致。这种物理引导的公式化方法提高了预测精度、长期稳定性，以及在不同空间分辨率和时间预测设置下的鲁棒性。针对调幅分解的大量实验表明，与纯数据驱动基线相比，引入物理引导的残差正则化能够更忠实地再现微观组织形貌、统计特征和演化趋势。该框架在保持全卷积架构的可扩展性和计算效率的同时，弥合了高保真物理模拟与数据驱动代理建模之间的差距，为数字孪生驱动的微观组织演化预测提供了可靠且高效的代理建模步骤。

英文原始摘要: Understanding and predicting microstructure evolution is central to materials design, yet purely data-driven spatiotemporal learning models often suffer from limited physical consistency and degraded long-term prediction accuracy. In this work, we introduce a physics-guided fully convolutional spatiotemporal learning framework for microstructure evolution prediction. Unlike prior self-supervised approaches, the proposed method explicitly incorporates governing physical equations into the training objective, thereby encouraging the learned dynamics to remain consistent with known thermodynamic and kinetic laws. This physics-guided formulation improves predictive accuracy, long-horizon stability, and robustness across spatial resolutions and temporal prediction settings. Extensive experiments for spinodal decomposition demonstrate that incorporating physics-guided residual regularization leads to more faithful reproduction of microstructural morphology, statistics, and evolution trends compared with purely data-driven baselines. The proposed framework preserves the scalability and computational efficiency of fully convolutional architectures while bridging the gap between high-fidelity physics-based simulations and data-driven surrogate modeling, offering a reliable and efficient surrogate-modeling step toward digital-twin-enabled microstructure evolution prediction.

<details>
  <summary>更多信息</summary>

研究动机: 具有记忆效应的随机模型自然产生时滞FBSDE系统，但时滞引入的系数对过去轨道的依赖及非马尔可夫结构带来了额外的分析挑战，需要发展新的渐近分析工具。

主要方法: 研究由小噪声参数驱动的扰动时滞FBSDE，在对系数施加适当假设下，先建立解过程的依分布收敛性，再证明几乎必然收敛到确定性极限系统，最终导出大偏差原理。

实验 / 验证: 本文为理论研究，无数值实验；核心论证包括依分布收敛和几乎必然收敛的严格证明，以及大偏差原理的推导。

主要结果: 证明了当扰动参数趋于零时解过程依分布收敛且几乎必然收敛到确定性极限系统的解，并由此导出了解过程的大偏差原理。

结论: 本文将Cruzeiro、Gomes和Zhang（2014）的经典完全耦合FBSDE渐近分析推广至时滞框架，补充了弱耦合时滞系统的研究，并首次为完全耦合时滞FBSDE建立了大偏差原理。

局限 / 后续问题: 

中文摘要: 我们研究了一类具有时滞生成元的完全耦合前向-后向随机微分方程解的渐近行为。此类系统自然地出现在具有记忆效应的随机模型中，并构成对经典完全耦合FBSDE框架的重要推广。由于系数依赖于解过程的过去轨道以及由此产生的非马尔可夫结构，时滞的引入带来了额外的分析困难。在对系数施加适当假设的条件下，我们研究了由小噪声参数驱动的扰动时滞FBSDE的渐近性质。我们首先建立了当扰动参数趋于零时相应解过程的依分布收敛性。随后证明了解过程几乎必然收敛到相应确定性极限系统的解。作为这些渐近结果的推论，我们导出了解过程的大偏差原理。我们的结果将Cruzeiro、Gomes和Zhang（2014）的渐近分析从经典完全耦合FBSDE框架推广到了时滞框架，并补充了关于弱耦合时滞前向-后向系统的现有工作。据我们所知，这些结果首次为具有时滞生成元的完全耦合前向-后向随机微分方程建立了大偏差原理。

英文原始摘要: We investigate the asymptotic behavior of solutions to a class of fully coupled forward-backward stochastic differential equations with time-delayed generators. Such systems arise naturally in stochastic models with memory effects and constitute a significant extension of the classical fully coupled FBSDE framework. The presence of delay introduces additional analytical difficulties due to the dependence of the coefficients on the past trajectories of the solution processes and the resulting non-Markovian structure. Under suitable assumptions on the coefficients, we study the asymptotic properties of a perturbed delayed FBSDE driven by a small noise parameter. We first establish the convergence in distribution of the associated solution processes as the perturbation parameter tends to zero. We then prove almost sure convergence towards the solution of the corresponding deterministic limiting system. As a consequence of these asymptotic results, we derive a large deviation principle for the solution processes. Our results extend the asymptotic analysis of Cruzeiro, Gomes and Zhang (2014) from the classical fully coupled FBSDE setting to the delayed framework, and complement existing works on weakly coupled delayed forward-backward systems. They provide, to the best of our knowledge, the first large deviation principle for fully coupled forward-backward stochastic differential equations with delayed generators.

An important example of such a process is the dynamics of the carbon content of a forest whose deterministic growth is interrupted by natural disasters (fires, droughts, insect outbreaks, etc.).

*Qinghui Chen,Zekai Zhang,Hailong Liu,Jinglin Zhang,Cong Bai*

主要创新点: 提出KFTD网络，通过将插值与预测解耦的两阶段范式，结合Koopman线性空间映射与傅里叶分析实现任意子步长连续时间插值，并引入DPP损失以端到端方式支持任意PDE约束。


<details>
  <summary>更多信息</summary>

研究动机: 海洋预报对气候监测和灾害预警至关重要，但现有方法在计算效率和物理一致性方面存在不足，亟需一种既能高效建模复杂动力系统又能保证物理一致性的连续时间预报框架。

主要方法: 将非线性动力学映射到Koopman线性空间，利用傅里叶分析实现连续时间插值，轻量级残差网络消费高保真中间状态生成最终预报；引入DPP损失以端到端方式施加任意PDE约束；避免扩散模型的多步噪声采样，直接在连续时间中演化系统。

实验 / 验证: 在四个海洋数据集上进行实验验证，包括SST（海表温度）等，与MCVD等基线方法进行对比。

主要结果: MSE平均降低5.6%（SST最高降低12.7%），计算速度提升4倍，效率比MCVD提高76.25%。

结论: KFTD网络通过解耦插值与预测、Koopman线性空间映射和傅里叶分析，实现了高效且物理一致的连续时间海洋时空预报，在精度和效率上均优于现有方法。

中文摘要: 准确的海洋预报对气候监测和灾害预警至关重要。然而，海洋时空预报面临建模复杂动力系统和确保计算效率的双重挑战。我们提出了Koopman傅里叶时间可微（KFTD）网络，这是一种时间连续的两阶段范式，将插值与预测解耦，以实现高效且可扩展的时空建模。我们将复杂非线性动力学映射到Koopman线性空间，并利用傅里叶分析实现任意子步长的连续时间插值。一个轻量级残差网络利用高保真中间状态生成最终预报。与扩散模型不同，KFTD消除了多步噪声采样，直接在连续时间中演化系统，实现了4倍的计算加速。我们进一步引入了DPP损失，以端到端方式支持任意PDE约束，打破了纯数据驱动方法的物理一致性瓶颈。在四个海洋数据集上的实验结果证实，我们的连续时间框架将MSE平均降低5.6%（SST最高降低12.7%），效率比MCVD提高76.25%。

英文原始摘要: Accurate oceanic forecasting is critical for climate monitoring and disaster early warning. However, ocean spatiotemporal forecasting encounters the double challenges of modeling complex dynamical systems and ensuring computational efficiency. We present Koopman Fourier Time-Differentiable (KFTD) Network, a time continuous twostage paradigm that decouples interpolation from prediction to achieve efficient and scalable spatiotemporal modeling. We map complex nonlinear dynamics into the Koopman linear space and exploit Fourier analysis to enable continuous time interpolation at arbitrary sub-steps. A lightweight residual network consumes the high fidelity intermediate states to yield the final forecast. Unlike diffusion models, KFTD eliminates multi step noise sampling and directly evolves the system in continuous time, yielding a 4 computational speedup. We further introduce a DPP Loss that supports arbitrary PDE constraints in an endtoend manner, breaking the physical consistency bottleneck of pure data-driven approaches. Empirical results on four ocean datasets confirm that our continuous time framework reduces MSE by an average of 5.6% (up to 12.7% for SST) and improves efficiency over MCVD by 76.25%.

### [116] [Geometry-Aware Anisotropic Boundary Correction for Aerodynamic Simulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09963v1)
*Xin Zhang,Yipeng Huang,Shu Jiang,Zhenzhong Wang,Min Jiang*

主分类: 数值计算与科学计算

一句话结论: 提出GeoABC框架，利用边界几何对各向异性近壁流动进行方向感知校正，显著降低神经算子的近边界误差。

研究问题: 传统神经算子各向同性地处理边界区域，未能建模空气动力学中近壁面切向流动传播与法向物理量约束的各向异性物理行为，导致近边界预测精度不足。

主要创新点: 提出几何条件的各向异性边界校正框架GeoABC，将边界几何从静态输入特征转化为结构先验，通过方向感知的边界校正调制神经算子中间表示，显式建模切向与法向的差异化物理行为。


<details>
  <summary>更多信息</summary>

研究动机: 空气动力学仿真中近边界流动具有各向异性：切向流动沿壁面传播，法向物理量受壁面约束，而现有神经算子忽略这一物理特性，导致近壁区域预测误差较大，限制了高保真仿真的实现。

主要方法: GeoABC利用边界几何信息，在神经算子的中间表示中引入方向感知的边界校正，将边界几何作为结构先验调制物理预测，从而显式区分切向和法向的物理行为差异。

实验 / 验证: 在二维翼型和三维汽车两类空气动力学任务上进行实验，将GeoABC与多种神经算子骨干网络结合，评估近边界预测精度。

主要结果: GeoABC在多种骨干网络上一致提升性能，近边界相对L2误差平均降低约38%，有效缩小了主流神经算子共有的结构性近壁差距。

结论: GeoABC通过几何条件的各向异性边界校正，显著提升了神经算子在近边界区域的预测精度，推动神经算子向高保真空气动力学仿真方向发展。

局限 / 后续问题: 

中文摘要: 空气动力学仿真是工程外形设计的关键环节，其中表面压力系数等核心量高度依赖于固体边界附近的流动动力学。神经算子为昂贵的计算流体力学（CFD）求解器提供了高效替代方案。然而，传统方法对各向同性地处理边界区域，未能考虑沿边界的不同物理行为。实际上，空气动力学过程表现出各向异性：沿切向方向，流动沿壁面传播；沿法向方向，物理量受壁面约束。为了显式建模这些不同的物理行为，我们提出了GeoABC，一种几何条件的各向异性边界校正框架。GeoABC利用边界几何信息，将方向感知的边界校正引入神经算子的中间表示中，将边界几何从静态输入特征转变为调制物理预测的结构先验。在二维翼型和三维汽车任务上，GeoABC持续适配多种神经算子骨干网络，将近边界相对L2误差平均降低约38%，缩小了主流神经算子共有的结构性近壁差距，推动神经算子向高保真空气动力学仿真迈进。

英文原始摘要: Aerodynamic simulation is a key component of engineering shape design, where core quantities such as the surface pressure coefficient strongly depend on flow dynamics near solid boundaries. Neural operators provide an efficient alternative to expensive Computational Fluid Dynamics (CFD) solvers. However, conventional methods treat the boundary region isotropically, failing to account for the distinct physical behaviors along the boundaries. In reality, the aerodynamic process exhibits anisotropy: along the tangential direction, flow propagates along the wall; along the normal direction, physical quantities are constrained by the wall. To explicitly model the distinct physical behaviors, we propose GeoABC, a geometry-conditioned anisotropic boundary correction framework. GeoABC leverages the boundary geometries to introduce direction-aware boundary correction into the intermediate representations of neural operators, transforming boundary geometry from static input features into a structural prior that modulates physical prediction. On 2D airfoil and 3D car tasks, GeoABC consistently adapts to multiple neural operator backbones, reducing near-boundary relative $L_2$ error by $\sim$38\% on average, narrowing the structural near-wall gap shared by mainstream neural operators, and advancing neural operators toward high-fidelity aerodynamic simulation.

### [117] [From Landau Equation and Large Deviations to Efficient Simulations of Dynamical Fluctuations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21318v1)
*Anwar El Rhirhayi,Jean-Baptiste Fouvry,Julien Barré*

一句话结论: 基于大偏差理论提出Langevin方程组，在恢复Landau平均动力学的同时精确刻画有限N系统的动力学涨落。

研究问题: 确定性Landau方程虽然成功描述了有限N系统的平均长期演化，但从根本上忽略了动力学涨落，无法刻画不同实现之间的统计涨落。

主要创新点: 基于大偏差理论构建了一组物理自洽的Langevin方程，在弱双体偏转极限下从Rostoker原理严格推导，同时恢复平均Landau动力学和涨落。

  <summary>更多信息</summary>

研究动机: 长程相互作用有限N系统的动力学涨落被Landau方程忽略，缺乏一个既能恢复平均动力学又能精确描述涨落的统一理论框架。

主要方法: 利用大偏差理论，从Rostoker原理出发，在弱双体偏转极限下推导出一组Langevin方程，使其同时包含平均Landau动力学项和涨落项。

实验 / 验证: 通过专门设计的直接N体模拟对所提出的Langevin方程进行广泛验证，比较平均动力学与涨落的统计性质。

主要结果: Langevin方程与直接N体模拟之间表现出极高的一致性，验证了该方程组在恢复平均动力学和刻画涨落方面的准确性。

结论: 所提出的Langevin方程组为有限N长程相互作用系统提供了一个物理自洽的动力学描述，同时准确捕捉平均演化和涨落。

局限 / 后续问题: 

中文摘要: （确定性的）Landau方程描述了动力学热的长程相互作用有限N系统的平均长期演化。尽管该方程取得了成功，但它从根本上忽略了动力学涨落。基于大偏差理论，我们提出了一组物理自洽的Langevin方程，能够同时恢复Landau平均动力学并精确刻画不同实现之间的相应涨落。我们特别展示了在弱双体偏转极限下，如何从Rostoker原理推导出这些Langevin方程。我们通过专门设计的直接N体模拟对这些方程进行了广泛验证，结果显示出极高的一致性。

英文原始摘要: The (deterministic) Landau equation captures the mean long-term evolution of dynamically hot long-range interacting finite-$N$ systems. Though successful, this kinetic equation fundamentally ignores dynamical fluctuations. Building upon Large Deviation Theory, we present a physically-consistent system of Langevin equations that simultaneously recovers the mean Landau dynamics and accurately captures the corresponding fluctuations among different realizations. We show in particular how these Langevin equations can be derived from Rostoker's principle in the limit of weak two-body deflections. We extensively validate these equations against tailored direct $N$-body simulations, showing an exquisite level of agreement.

### [118] [Temporal Difference Learning for Diffusion Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15048v1)
*Qizhen Ying,Yangchen Pan,Victor Adrian Prisacariu,Junfeng Wen*

一句话结论: 提出时序差分目标强制扩散模型去噪轨迹的跨时间一致性，显著提升少步采样质量。

研究问题: 扩散模型的训练目标仅关注单个时间步的局部去噪，不强制去噪轨迹上各步预测之间的跨时间一致性，导致少步采样器性能下降。

主要创新点: 将扩散过程重新表述为马尔可夫奖励过程，把去噪转化为强化学习中的策略评估问题，从而推导出统一的时序差分（TD）训练目标，惩罚去噪路径上多步预测的不一致性。


<details>
  <summary>更多信息</summary>

研究动机: 现有扩散模型训练目标缺乏跨时间一致性约束，在少步采样场景下性能退化明显，需要一种方法来强制去噪轨迹上的预测一致性。

主要方法: 将扩散过程建模为马尔可夫奖励过程，将去噪视为强化学习策略评估问题，推导出适用于离散和连续时间扩散的统一TD目标；并提出基于样本的重加权方法稳定训练。

实验 / 验证: 在多种扩散生成模型上验证TD训练效果，使用FID评估样本质量，特别关注少步采样场景；并进行消融研究验证成对损失重加权、正则化权重和单步跨度等设计选择。

主要结果: TD训练显著改善FID指标，在采样步数较少时优势更为明显，适用于低计算预算场景。

结论: TD方法可作为通用即插即用模块，强制跨时间一致性并提升不同扩散模型的生成质量。

局限 / 后续问题: 

中文摘要: 扩散模型通常使用专注于单个时间步（或相邻时间步对）的局部去噪目标进行训练，这些目标不强制去噪轨迹上预测之间的跨时间一致性。这种跨时间一致性的缺乏会降低性能，尤其是对于少步采样器。我们引入了一个时序差分（TD）目标，用于惩罚模型沿去噪路径多步进展的不一致性。通过将扩散过程重新表述为马尔可夫奖励过程，并将去噪转化为强化学习中的策略评估问题，我们推导出一种统一的TD方法，适用于离散时间和连续时间扩散公式。我们进一步提出了一种有原则的基于样本的重加权方法来稳定训练。在实验中，我们表明使用TD训练可以显著改善以FID衡量的样本质量，当采样步数较少时优势更加明显，突出了其在低计算预算场景下的实用价值。我们提供了消融研究来验证设计选择，包括成对损失重加权、正则化权重和单步跨度。总体而言，我们的TD方法可以作为一个通用的即插即用模块，强制跨时间一致性并改善不同扩散生成模型的生成质量。

英文原始摘要: Diffusion models are typically trained with objectives that focus on local denoising targets at individual time steps (or adjacent pairs), which do not enforce consistency between predictions along the denoising trajectory. This lack of cross-time consistency can degrade performance, especially for few-step samplers. We introduce a temporal difference (TD) objective that penalizes inconsistency of the model's multi-step progress along the denoising path. By reformulating the diffusion process as a Markov reward process and casting denoising as a policy evaluation problem in reinforcement learning, we derive a unified TD approach that applies to both discrete- and continuous-time diffusion formulations. We further propose a principled sample-based reweighting method that stabilizes training. Empirically, we show that using our TD training can significantly improve sample quality measured by FID, with stronger advantages when the number of sampling steps is small, highlighting its practical utility under low-computation-budget scenarios. We provide ablation studies to justify our design choices, including pairwise loss reweighting, regularization weight, and one-step stride. Overall, our TD approach can be a general drop-in that enforces cross-time consistency and improves generation quality across different diffusion generative models.

Recognizing dragon-king events as regime-generated outliers and incorporating non-normal transient amplification are essential, as is accounting for organizational concealment of risk. A geopolitical crisis observatory would diagnose when systems enter states of heightened susceptibility to cascading disruptions. While state actors are already developing such observatories for strategic purposes, media institutions remain largely reactive. This gap creates a strategic opportunity: leveraging open data and AI embedded within the complex-systems framework developed above, media organizations could transform journalism from reporting to diagnosis, delivering early-warning indicators, scenario-based risk maps, and transparent, data-driven narratives within a new Geopolitical Risk Intelligence Platform.

### [120] [Loop Current Extension as an Effective Delayed Dynamical System](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06844v1)
*Francisco J. Beron-Vera,María J. Olascoaga,Philippe Miron*

研究问题: 环流变率是否可以归约为简化的低维动力学描述，这一问题在数十年研究后仍不明确。

主要创新点: 将延迟坐标表示与岭回归、多层感知机和SINDy三种机器学习方法结合，从卫星高度计数据中学习紧凑的延迟演化映射，揭示环流延伸的低维动力学结构。


<details>
  <summary>更多信息</summary>

研究动机: 环流是墨西哥湾主导环流特征，其延伸、收缩和涡旋脱落变率显著，但能否用简化动力学描述尚不清楚，需要数据驱动方法来探索其可降维性。

主要方法: 基于卫星高度计观测的环流延伸时间序列构建延迟坐标表示，分别应用岭回归、多层感知机预测和非线性动力学稀疏辨识（SINDy）学习延迟演化映射，并结合尤卡坦海峡入流、佛罗里达海峡出流等物理诊断进行信息评估。

实验 / 验证: 利用卫星高度计观测数据，在30至90天超前时效下比较三种方法的预测技巧与持续性预报基准，分析延迟状态维度饱和特性，评估SINDy映射在递归迭代下的稳定性，并检验物理诊断变量是否能提供额外独立预测信息。

主要结果: 三种方法预测技巧在30至90天超前时效均超过持续性预报，且仅需少量延迟坐标。岭回归预测技巧随延迟维度饱和；神经网络仅带来适度改进；SINDy识别出涉及约两周至数月季节内记忆尺度的稀疏稳定演化映射。物理诊断虽含预测信息，但在纳入延迟环流状态后不提供额外独立信息。

结论: 环流延伸可被视为在有效低维延迟动力系统上演化的可观测变量，其大部分可预测变率可从少量延迟观测重建并以紧凑延迟演化映射表示。

局限 / 后续问题: 

中文摘要: 环流是墨西哥湾的主要环流特征，表现出与北向延伸、收缩和涡旋脱落相关的显著变率。尽管已研究数十年，这种变率在多大程度上可归约为简化动力学描述仍不清楚。我们利用由卫星高度计观测的环流延伸数据构建的延迟坐标表示来研究这一问题。对延伸时间序列应用岭回归、多层感知机预测和非线性动力学稀疏辨识（SINDy）来学习延迟演化映射。预测技巧在30至90天的超前时效内持续超过持续性预报，且仅需少量延迟坐标。岭回归显示随延迟状态维度趋于饱和，表明大部分预测信息包含在紧凑表示中。神经网络预测提供了适度的额外改进，而延迟SINDy识别出涉及季节内记忆尺度（约两周至数月）的稀疏演化映射，该映射在递归迭代下保持稳定。与尤卡坦海峡入流、佛罗里达海峡出流、通道几何形状和加勒比北部涡度相关的物理诊断包含预测信息，但一旦纳入延迟环流状态，便不再提供额外的独立状态信息。这些结果支持将环流延伸解释为在有效低维延迟动力系统上演化的可观测变量。相当一部分可预测变率可从少量延迟观测中重建，并通过紧凑的延迟演化映射表示。

英文原始摘要: The Loop Current is the dominant circulation feature of the Gulf of Mexico and exhibits pronounced variability associated with northward extension, retraction, and eddy shedding. Despite decades of study, the extent to which this variability admits a reduced dynamical description remains unclear.
  We investigate this question using delayed-coordinate representations constructed from satellite-altimetry observations of Loop Current extension. Ridge regression, multilayer perceptron forecasting, and Sparse Identification of Nonlinear Dynamics (SINDy) are applied to learn delayed evolution maps from the extension time series. Forecast skill consistently exceeds persistence at lead times of 30--90 days while requiring only a small number of delayed coordinates. Ridge regression reveals saturation with delayed-state dimension, indicating that much of the predictive information is contained within a compact representation. Neural-network forecasts provide modest additional improvements, while delayed SINDy identifies sparse evolution maps involving intraseasonal memory scales, from approximately two weeks to a few months, that remain stable under recursive iteration. Physical diagnostics associated with Yucatan Channel inflow, Florida Straits outflow, gateway geometry, and northern Caribbean vorticity contain predictive information but do not provide additional independent state information once the delayed Loop Current state is included.
  These results support the interpretation of Loop Current extension as an observable evolving on an effective low-dimensional delayed dynamical system. A substantial fraction of the predictable variability can be reconstructed from a small number of delayed observations and represented through compact delayed evolution maps.

*Chen Chao,Zixiao Ma,Ziang Zhang*

主分类: 数值计算与科学计算

期刊:

一句话结论: 提出基于DAE-PINN的电网侧数据中心负荷韧性评估框架，实现快速且物理一致的恢复策略筛选。

研究问题: 现有静态服务状态或能量指标无法捕捉数据中心断开和分级重新接入所引发的快速电压和频率动态，且传统方法依赖详细的数据中心内部模型，难以从电网侧高效评估韧性。

主要创新点: 提出基于隐式后向欧拉残差的无监督DAE-PINN，联合预测动态与代数状态并保持网络代数一致性，结合归一化多阶段韧性指标，在无需数据中心内部模型的前提下实现电网侧韧性评估与恢复策略筛选。


<details>
  <summary>更多信息</summary>

研究动机: 大型数据中心负荷的断开与分级重新接入会引发快速电压和频率动态，现有韧性指标无法捕捉这些动态，亟需一种仅依赖电网侧信息的物理驱动评估方法。

主要方法: 构建电网侧物理信息韧性评估框架，开发基于隐式后向欧拉残差的无监督DAE-PINN联合预测动态和代数状态，利用归一化多阶段韧性指标量化扰动、降级和恢复期影响，并在安全约束下筛选重新接入时机与负荷爬坡策略。

实验 / 验证: 在改进的IEEE 33节点馈线上进行案例研究，验证DAE-PINN轨迹跟踪精度和计算效率，并分析不同扰动规模、数据中心位置和重新接入策略对韧性指标的影响。

主要结果: DAE-PINN准确跟踪数值DAE解并大幅降低重复恢复筛选的计算时间；所提指标有效区分扰动规模、数据中心位置和重新接入策略的影响，揭示恢复速度与暂态韧性损失的权衡。

结论: 所提框架无需数据中心内部模型即可从电网侧准确评估数据中心负荷的韧性影响，为恢复策略筛选提供了高效且物理一致的工具。

局限 / 后续问题: 

中文摘要: 大型数据中心负荷给电力系统带来了新的韧性挑战，因为其断开和分级重新接入会引发快速的电压和频率动态，而这些动态无法被基于静态服务状态或能量的指标所捕捉。本文提出了一种电网侧的、物理信息驱动的韧性评估框架，该框架仅使用电网侧动态模型和可观测的扰动后轨迹来评估这些事件，无需详细的数据中心内部模型。开发了一种基于隐式后向欧拉残差的无监督微分代数方程物理信息神经网络（DAE-PINN），用于联合预测动态状态和代数状态，在强制网络代数一致性的同时实现重复的扰动后轨迹评估。随后采用归一化的多阶段韧性指标来量化扰动、降级状态和恢复期的影响，并在安全约束下筛选数据中心重新接入时机和负荷爬坡策略。在改进的IEEE 33节点馈线上的案例研究表明，所提出的DAE-PINN能准确跟踪数值DAE解，并大幅减少重复恢复筛选的计算时间。所提出的指标能够区分扰动规模、数据中心位置和重新接入策略的影响，揭示了恢复速度与暂态韧性损失之间的权衡关系。

英文原始摘要: Large data center loads introduce new resilience challenges to power systems because their disconnection and staged reconnection can induce fast voltage and frequency dynamics that are not captured by static service-status or energy-based metrics. This paper proposes a utility-side, physics-informed resilience assessment framework that evaluates these events using only grid-side dynamic models and observable post-disturbance trajectories, without requiring detailed internal data center models. An unsupervised differential algebraic equation-physics informed neural network (DAE-PINN) based on an implicit backward Euler residual is developed to jointly predict dynamic and algebraic states, enabling repeated post-disturbance trajectory evaluation while enforcing network algebraic consistency. Normalized multi-phase resilience metrics are then used to quantify disturbance, degraded-state, and restoration-period impacts and to screen data center reconnection timing and load-ramping strategies under security constraints. Case studies on a modified IEEE 33-bus feeder show that the proposed DAE-PINN accurately tracks numerical DAE solutions and substantially reduces computation time in repeated restoration screening. The proposed metrics distinguish the effects of disturbance size, data center location, and reconnection strategy, revealing the trade-off between restoration speed and transient resilience loss.

</details>


### [122] [A Moment-Based Eulerian Method for Variance-Based Finite-Time Lyapunov Exponent Computation in Stochastic Flows](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19681v1)
*Shingyu Leung*

一句话结论: 用单个协方差张量场替代逐点Fokker-Planck求解，高效近似小噪声下的vFTLE。

研究问题: 现有基于PDF的vFTLE计算方法需要为每个初始点求解Fokker-Planck方程，在密集网格上计算代价过高，难以高效应用。

主要创新点: 提出基于矩的欧拉近似方法，将逐点Fokker-Planck方程求解替换为单个对称协方差张量场的输运-反应方程演化，在d维空间仅需d(d+1)/2个标量场，同时通过特征向量保留随机扩散的方向信息。


<details>
  <summary>更多信息</summary>

研究动机: 在密集网格上计算vFTLE诊断量时，逐点求解Fokker-Planck方程的计算成本过高，亟需一种高效且保留方向信息的替代方法。

主要方法: 从确定性流附近的随机轨迹展开出发，推导主导随机位移的封闭协方差方程；将其嵌入物理空间得到对称协方差张量场的欧拉输运-反应方程；在确定性到达位置评估该张量场以恢复各初始点的协方差，并由其最大特征值定义基于矩的vFTLE。

实验 / 验证: 摘要中未提及具体数值实验，主要为理论分析，包括小噪声极限下与基于PDF的vFTLE的主导阶一致性证明，以及与标量随机灵敏度和确定性FTLE关系的讨论。

主要结果: 方法在小噪声极限下与基于PDF的vFTLE在主导阶上一致；在d维空间仅需d(d+1)/2个标量场；通过特征向量保留随机扩散方向信息；无过程噪声时可恢复确定性FTLE（至多差加性常数），连续过程噪声产生时间积分变形协方差。

结论: 所提基于矩的欧拉方法为小噪声情形下的vFTLE计算提供了高效替代方案，兼具理论一致性和方向信息保留能力，并揭示了过程噪声扩散与确定性变形之间的内在联系。

局限 / 后续问题: 方法仅适用于小噪声情形；摘要中未提及数值验证实验，仅有理论一致性分析。

中文摘要: 基于方差的有限时间Lyapunov指数（vFTLEs）通过测量随机到达位置的协方差，提供了确定性FTLE的随机类比。现有的基于PDF的公式通过为每个初始点求解Fokker-Planck方程来计算该协方差，当需要在密集网格上获取该诊断量时，计算代价高昂。本文在小噪声情形下发展了一种基于矩的vFTLE欧拉近似方法。从确定性流附近的随机轨迹展开出发，我们推导了主导随机位移的封闭协方差方程。通过将逐轨迹的协方差动力学嵌入物理空间，我们获得了对称协方差张量场的欧拉输运-反应方程。每个初始点对应的协方差通过在确定性到达位置处评估该张量场来恢复，然后基于矩的vFTLE由其最大特征值定义。所提方法用单个协方差张量场的演化替代了一族Fokker-Planck方程的求解，在d维空间中仅需d(d+1)/2个标量场。该方法还通过协方差张量的特征向量保留了方向信息，从而可以可视化随机扩散的主导方向。我们建立了该方法与基于PDF的vFTLE在小噪声极限下的主导阶一致性，阐明了其与标量随机灵敏度之间的关系，并展示了同一协方差方程如何将过程噪声扩散与确定性变形联系起来。特别地，当不存在过程噪声时，从各向同性初始协方差出发可恢复确定性FTLE（至多差一个加性常数），而连续过程噪声则产生时间积分的变形协方差。

英文原始摘要: Variance-based finite-time Lyapunov exponents (vFTLEs) provide a stochastic analogue of deterministic FTLE by measuring the covariance of stochastic arrival locations. Existing PDF-based formulations compute this covariance by solving a Fokker--Planck equation for each initial point, which becomes expensive when the diagnostic is required on a dense grid. In this work, we develop a moment-based Eulerian approximation to vFTLE in the small-noise regime. Starting from a stochastic trajectory expansion about the deterministic flow, we derive a closed covariance equation for the leading stochastic displacement. By embedding this trajectory-wise covariance dynamics into physical space, we obtain an Eulerian transport--reaction equation for a symmetric covariance tensor field. The covariance associated with each initial point is recovered by evaluating this tensor field at the deterministic arrival location, and a moment-based vFTLE is then defined from its largest eigenvalue. The proposed method replaces a family of Fokker--Planck solves by the evolution of a single covariance tensor field, requiring only $d(d+1)/2$ scalar fields in $d$ dimensions. It also retains directional information through the eigenvectors of the covariance tensor, allowing the dominant directions of stochastic spreading to be visualized. We establish the leading-order consistency of the method with PDF-based vFTLE in the small-noise limit, clarify its relation to scalar stochastic sensitivity, and show how the same covariance equation connects process-noise spreading with deterministic deformation. In particular, deterministic FTLE is recovered, up to an additive constant, from an isotropic initial covariance when no process noise is present, while continuous process noise produces a time-integrated deformation covariance.

</details>

### [124] [OrthoReg: Orthogonal Regularization for Hybrid Symbolic-Neural Dynamical Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19145v1)
*Till Richter,Niki Kilbertus*

主分类: 数值计算与科学计算

来源: arxiv

期刊: 

DOI: 

免费全文: [arXiv abstract](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19145v1), [arXiv pdf](https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.19145v1), [Google Scholar search](https://scholar.google.com/scholar?q=OrthoReg%3A+Orthogonal+Regularization+for+Hybrid+Symbolic-Neural+Dynamical+Systems++free+full+text+pdf)

一句话结论: 提出OrthoReg正交正则化方法，防止混合模型中神经成分重复学习符号结构。

研究问题: 混合动力系统建模中，神经组件会重新学习符号组件已表达的机理结构，导致模型冗余且不可解释；而现有基于L2正则化的方法在符号结构通过稀疏发现学习时投影论证失效，无法阻止这种重叠。

主要创新点: 提出OrthoReg（正交正则化），直接惩罚符号组件与神经组件之间的重叠，确保两者形成互补分解而非冗余重复。


<details>
  <summary>更多信息</summary>

研究动机: 混合模型中神经部分倾向于吸收符号结构已能表达的信息，尤其在符号结构从数据中自动发现时更为严重，标准L2正则化在此场景下失效，亟需新方法约束组件间的重叠。

主要方法: 设计正交正则化项，直接惩罚符号组件与神经残差之间的重叠，使符号部分捕获基函数库可表达的结构，神经部分仅捕获剩余部分，实现互补分解。

实验 / 验证: 在具有部分库失配的基准动力系统上进行实验，评估符号恢复能力和分布外行为表现。

主要结果: OrthoReg在符号恢复和分布外行为方面均取得改善。

结论: OrthoReg通过直接惩罚符号与神经组件间的重叠，实现了互补的模型分解，有效防止符号结构被神经残差吸收，提升了符号恢复和泛化能力。

局限 / 后续问题: 

中文摘要: 动力系统是建模自然世界的基础，然而建模它们涉及一个持续的权衡：人工设定的机理模型在设计上具有可解释性，但往往过于简单且存在误设；相比之下，灵活的数据驱动神经方法缺乏物理洞察。混合建模旨在兼取两者之长，将预设或符号化的物理组件与灵活的神经网络相结合。然而，一个关键挑战是神经组件可能重新学习机理部分，产生冗余且不可解释的模型，尤其是当符号结构本身从数据中发现时。基于标准$L^2$正则化的现有方法依赖于一个投影论证，当符号组件通过稀疏发现学习时该论证失效，使得神经增强与符号结构发生重叠。我们提出了\textbf{OrthoReg}（正交正则化），直接惩罚符号组件与神经组件之间的重叠，防止符号结构被神经残差吸收。这产生了一种互补分解：符号部分捕获库所能表达的内容，神经部分捕获剩余内容。在具有部分库失配的基准动力系统上，OrthoReg改善了符号恢复和分布外行为。

英文原始摘要: Dynamical systems are fundamental to modeling the natural world, yet modeling them involves a persistent trade-off: manually prescribed mechanistic models are interpretable by design but often overly simplistic and misspecified; in contrast, flexible data-driven neural methods lack physical insight. Hybrid modeling aims for the best of both worlds by combining a prescribed or symbolic, physics-based component with a flexible neural network. A critical challenge, however, is that the neural component may relearn mechanistic parts, yielding redundant and uninterpretable models, especially when the symbolic structure itself is discovered from data. Existing methods based on standard $L^2$ regularization rely on a projection argument that breaks when the symbolic component is learned through sparse discovery, allowing the neural augmentation to overlap with symbolic structure. We introduce \textbf{OrthoReg} (Orthogonal Regularization), which directly penalizes overlap between the symbolic and neural components, preventing symbolic structure from being absorbed by the neural residual. This yields a complementary decomposition: the symbolic part captures what the library can express, and the neural part captures what remains. On benchmark dynamical systems with partial library mismatch, OrthoReg improves symbolic recovery and out-of-distribution behavior.

主要创新点: 提出了两种互补的随机表示方法：一是通过引入停止符号增广控制空间，将障碍项纳入运行支付的无穷时间域SDG；二是引入依赖对手控制过程的非预期停止策略，使停止分量与Elliott-Kalton策略框架兼容的混合控制-停止SDG。

  <summary>更多信息</summary>

研究动机: HJBI变分不等式在博弈论与最优控制中具有重要地位，建立其概率表示有助于从随机分析角度理解并求解双侧约束下的变分不等式问题。

主要方法: 第一种方法在无穷时间域随机递归微分博弈框架下扩充控制空间，将障碍项纳入运行支付；第二种方法利用BSDE定义随机终止时间支付，引入非预期停止策略。证明基于惩罚无穷时间域SDG、动态规划论证及反向半群稳定性估计。

实验 / 验证: 本文为理论研究，未涉及数值实验。

主要结果: 两种表示的下值函数和上值函数均被证明是对应双侧HJBI变分不等式的唯一有界粘性解。

结论: 通过两种互补的随机微分博弈框架，成功建立了双侧约束稳态HJBI变分不等式的概率表示，并证明了值函数与粘性解的等价性与唯一性。

局限 / 后续问题: 

中文摘要: 本文研究了具有双侧约束的稳态HJBI型变分不等式的概率表示。我们提供了两种互补的随机表示。第一种表示通过增广的无穷时间域双人零和随机微分博弈（SDG）获得。通过用两个额外的停止符号扩充控制空间，障碍项被纳入运行支付中。利用无穷时间域随机递归微分博弈的框架，我们证明了所得的下值函数和上值函数是对应HJBI变分不等式的唯一有界粘性解。第二种表示由双人零和混合控制-停止SDG给出。在此表述中，每个参与者同时选择连续控制和停止决策，支付由具有随机终止时间的BSDE定义。为使停止分量与Elliott-Kalton策略框架兼容，我们引入了依赖于对手控制过程的非预期停止策略。证明基于与各自值函数耦合的惩罚无穷时间域SDG，结合动态规划论证和反向半群的稳定性估计。我们证明了混合控制-停止博弈的值函数与双侧HJBI变分不等式的唯一有界粘性解一致。

英文原始摘要: In this paper, we study probabilistic representations for stationary HJBI-type variational inequalities with bilateral constraints. We provide two complementary stochastic representations.The first representation is obtained through an augmented infinite-horizon two-player zero-sum stochastic differential game (SDG). By enlarging the control spaces with two additional stopping symbols, the obstacle terms are incorporated into the running payoff. Using the framework of infinite-horizon stochastic recursive differential games, we show that the resulting lower and upper value functions are the unique bounded viscosity solutions of the corresponding HJBI variational inequalities. The second representation is given by a two-player zero-sum mixed control--stopping SDG. In this formulation, each player chooses both a continuous control and a stopping decision, and the payoff is defined by a BSDE with a random terminal time. To make the stopping component compatible with the Elliott--Kalton strategy framework, we introduce nonanticipative stopping strategies depending on the opponent's control process. The proof is based on penalized infinite-horizon SDGs coupled with their own value functions, together with dynamic programming arguments and stability estimates for backward semigroups. We prove that the value functions of the mixed control--stopping game coincide with the unique bounded viscosity solutions of the bilateral HJBI variational inequalities.

主要方法: 以多元Ornstein-Uhlenbeck过程为稳定不动点附近弛豫的典型线性模型，通过分析对数似然曲率沿稳定性方向的变化，推导估计精度与测量预算、信噪比及距临界性距离的解析关系。

实验 / 验证: 基于理论分析与解析推导，未涉及具体数值实验或实证数据分析。

主要结果: 可达到的精度由有效测量预算、信噪比和距临界性距离三因素共同决定；距临界性越近，最慢模式软化导致对数似然曲率变平，估计距离的相对不确定性发散；时间相关使有效独立观测数远低于名义样本数，当有效计数低于系统维度时推断崩溃，即使原始数据量看似充足。

结论: 存在一个在系统接近临界性时发散的最优采样间隔，该结果对复杂系统临界性检测的实验设计具有直接指导意义。

局限 / 后续问题: 分析基于线性模型（多元Ornstein-Uhlenbeck过程），对非线性系统的适用性未讨论；摘要未涉及实际数据验证。

中文摘要: 许多复杂系统，包括生态系统、神经回路和金融市场，被推断在不稳定性阈值附近运行，微小扰动即可传播至整个系统。这种接近性通常被认为具有功能优势，但也带来了一个跨领域共同问题：从有限且含噪声的记录中，能多精确地估计系统距该阈值的距离？我们以多元Ornstein-Uhlenbeck过程作为稳定不动点附近弛豫的典型线性模型，表明可达到的精度由三个因素决定：有效测量预算，由样本数相对于系统维度和采样间隔设定；信噪比，由确定性相互作用相对于随机驱动的幅度给出；以及距临界性的距离，它同时设定系统的相关时间并削弱前两个因素。当最慢动力学模式在阈值附近软化时，对数似然的曲率沿决定稳定性的方向变平，因此估计距离的相对不确定性在该距离趋零时发散。关键的是，不稳定性附近的时间相关使有效独立观测数远低于名义样本数，当该有效计数低于系统维度时推断即崩溃，即使原始数据量看似充足。一个直接后果是存在一个最优采样间隔，它在系统接近临界性时发散，对实验设计具有实际意义。

英文原始摘要: Many complex systems, including ecosystems, neural circuits, and financial markets, are inferred to operate close to a threshold of instability, at which a small perturbation can propagate across the entire system. This proximity is often interpreted as functionally advantageous, yet it poses a question common to all these fields: from a finite, noisy recording, how precisely can the distance of a system from that threshold be estimated? Using the multivariate Ornstein-Uhlenbeck process as the canonical linear model of relaxation near a stable fixed point, we show that the attainable precision is governed by three factors: an effective measurement budget, set by the number of samples relative to the system dimension and the sampling interval; the signal-to-noise ratio, given by the magnitude of deterministic interactions relative to stochastic forcing; and the distance to criticality, which simultaneously sets the system's correlation times and degrades both of the preceding factors. As the slowest dynamical mode softens near the threshold, the curvature of the log-likelihood flattens along the direction that determines stability, so that the relative uncertainty on the estimated distance diverges as that distance vanishes. Critically, temporal correlations near instability reduce the effective number of independent observations far below the nominal sample count, and inference breaks down when this effective count falls below the system dimension, even when the raw data volume appears sufficient.
  A direct consequence is the existence of an optimal sampling interval that diverges as the system approaches criticality, with practical implications for experimental design.

</details>

实验 / 验证: 在低维周期系统和混沌系统上进行了验证，并在一个高维示例中将方法应用于综合地球系统模型中的厄尔尼诺-南方涛动现象。

主要结果: 方法在所有示例中均发现了非平凡的最优扰动，这些扰动事后验证是自然的，且与期望的动力学操控目标（如提高频率或抑制相关性衰减）一致。

结论: 所提出的数据驱动框架能够有效发现非线性动力系统的最优线性响应扰动，适用于从低维到高维的多种系统，且所得扰动具有物理合理性。

局限 / 后续问题: 

中文摘要: 我们开发了一个数据驱动框架，用于估计非线性动力系统的最优线性响应。我们的方法基于对系统转移/Koopman算子的核平滑近似，这些近似由沿轨迹的（可能高维的）观测数据构建。将这些算子近似与Antown等人（2018, J. Stat. Phys., 170(6), 1051-1087）发展的理论相结合，我们提出了一个计算上可处理的优化问题，用于求解实现任意期望频谱操控的最优无穷小扰动。我们还引入了最优响应向量场的概念，用于可视化和物理解释系统在任意观测下对最优扰动的响应。我们的重点在于寻找能够最优地提高频率或最优地抑制与核平滑转移算子特征值相关联的近似周期或近似不变集的相关性衰减的扰动。我们通过低维周期和混沌系统的应用，以及一个涉及综合地球系统模型中厄尔尼诺-南方涛动的高维示例来说明我们的方法。在这些示例中，我们的方法发现了系统的非平凡最优扰动，这些扰动事后看来是自然的，并与期望的动力学目标一致。

英文原始摘要: We develop a data-driven framework for estimating optimal linear response of nonlinear dynamical systems. Our approach is based on kernel-smoothed approximations of the transfer/Koopman operators of the system, built from possibly high-dimensional observations along trajectories. Combining these operator approximations with the theory developed in [Antown et al. (2018), J. Stat. Phys., 170(6), 1051-1087], we formulate a computationally tractable optimization problem for the optimal infinitesimal perturbation realising any desired manipulation of the spectrum. We also introduce a notion of optimal-response vector fields for visualising, and physically interpreting, the system's response to the optimal perturbation under arbitrary observations.
  Our focus is on finding perturbations that optimally increase the frequency or optimally suppress the decay of correlations of almost-cycles or almost-invariant sets associated with the eigenvalues of the kernel-smoothed transfer operator. We illustrate our approach with applications to low-dimensional periodic and chaotic systems, as well as a high-dimensional example involving the El Nino Southern Oscillation in a comprehensive Earth system model. In these examples our approach discovers nontrivial optimal perturbations of the system, which are post hoc natural and consistent with the desired dynamical objectives.

  <summary>更多信息</summary>

研究动机: FPE在描述随机动力学系统PDF时间演化中至关重要，但传统方法难以高效处理一族初始条件下的解，且Dirac delta初始分布会导致映射奇异性和数值不稳定性，需要新的方法来克服这些困难。

主要方法: 利用Chapman-Kolmogorov方程将问题重新表述为近似转移PDF，采用线性化SDE的PDF作为归一化流基础分布以避免奇异性，结合PINN框架求解，并引入时间加权损失函数在因果性与训练难度间取得平衡。

主要结果: 所提方法能够有效且鲁棒地近似FPE的解算子，时间加权损失函数成功缓解了小时间尺度上的数值不稳定性。

结论: 基于条件归一化流的PINN框架结合线性化SDE基础分布和时间加权损失函数，为高效近似FPE解算子提供了有效且鲁棒的方法。

局限 / 后续问题: 

中文摘要: Fokker-Planck方程（FPE）在描述由随机动力学支配的系统概率密度函数（PDF）的时间演化中起着关键作用。在本工作中，我们提出了一种基于条件归一化流的物理信息神经网络（PINN）框架，用于高效近似FPE在一整族初始条件下的解算子。利用马尔可夫随机过程的Chapman-Kolmogorov方程，将该问题重新表述为近似从初始时刻以任意点为中心的Dirac质量出发的转移PDF。采用相关线性化随机微分方程（SDE）的PDF作为归一化流的基础分布，提供了对目标PDF的良好近似，特别是在小时间尺度上，从而避免了与Dirac delta初始分布相关的映射奇异性。此外，引入了时间加权损失函数以缓解小时间尺度上出现的数值不稳定性，在因果性和训练难度之间随时间推进实现平衡。展示了多种数值实验以说明所提方法的有效性和鲁棒性。

英文原始摘要: The Fokker-Planck equation (FPE) plays a pivotal role in describing the time evolution of probability density functions (PDFs) for systems governed by stochastic dynamics. In this work, we propose a conditional normalizing flow-based physics-informed neural network (PINN) framework for efficiently approximating the solution operator of the FPE for a whole range of initial conditions. Leveraging the Chapman-Kolmogorov equation for Markovian stochastic processes, the problem is reformulated into approximating a transition PDF starting at initial time from a Dirac mass centered at an arbitrary point. The PDF of an associated linearized stochastic differential equation (SDE) is employed as the base distribution for the normalizing flow, providing a good approximation of the target PDF, especially for small times, and thereby avoiding the singularity of the map associated with the Dirac delta initial distribution. Furthermore, a time-weighted loss function is introduced to mitigate numerical instabilities arising at small times, achieving a balance between causality and training difficulty as time progresses. A variety of numerical experiments are presented to illustrate the effectiveness and robustness of the proposed method.

英文原始摘要: We develop two implementations of the Event-Chain Monte Carlo (ECMC) algorithm for Yang-Mills $\mathrm{SU}(N)$ lattice gauge theories with the Wilson action. These algorithms consist in a succession of local ballistic updates intersped with stochastic events, resulting in an irreversible and rejection-free Markov process. The resulting dynamics satisfy global balance, ensuring the correct equilibrium distribution. The algorithms are formulated for general $\mathrm{SU}(N)$ Yang-Mills theories with Wilson action and implemented for the case $N=3$. Numerical tests on four-dimensional lattices show that standard gauge observables, such as the mean plaquette, agree with results obtained using conventional Monte Carlo algorithms. These results provide a first validation of ECMC as a viable sampling scheme for Yang-Mills lattice gauge theories.

### [130] [Randomized Optimal Switching Problem and Related Mirror Descent Flow](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12875v1)
*Yuchao Dong*

主分类: 数值计算与科学计算

来源: arxiv

期刊: 

DOI: 

免费全文: [arXiv abstract](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12875v1), [arXiv pdf](https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.12875v1), [Google Scholar search](https://scholar.google.com/scholar?q=Randomized+Optimal+Switching+Problem+and+Related+Mirror+Descent+Flow++free+full+text+pdf)

一句话结论: 提出连续时间最优切换问题的KL正则化随机化框架，通过镜像下降流实现收敛求解。

研究问题: 连续时间最优切换问题中缺乏有效的探索机制，且经典确定性切换控制难以直接应用于强化学习场景；同时，正则化后的问题缺乏高效的数值求解方法。

主要创新点: 将确定性切换控制松弛为由状态依赖生成元的连续时间马尔可夫链驱动的随机化框架，引入KL散度正则化，并在对偶对数策略空间中提出镜像下降流进行数值求解。


<details>
  <summary>更多信息</summary>

研究动机: 经典最优切换问题的确定性控制框架缺乏探索能力，无法直接适用于强化学习场景，需要通过随机化和正则化来引入探索机制。

主要方法: 将切换决策建模为连续时间马尔可夫链，在成本泛函中加入KL散度正则化；通过HJB系统分析证明值函数的正则性与最优Gibbs策略的显式形式；在对偶对数策略空间中构造镜像下降流，分析其适定性、单调性和收敛性。

实验 / 验证: 本文为理论分析工作，摘要中未涉及数值实验。

主要结果: 正则化值函数是HJB系统的唯一光滑解，最优策略为Gibbs策略；正则化值函数逼近经典最优值函数的误差为 $O(λ\log\frac{1}{λ})$；镜像下降流保证值函数单调递减，恒定温度调度下收敛速率为 $O(\frac{1}{e^{λs}-1}+λ\log\frac{1}{λ})$，退火调度下收敛速率为 $O(\frac{\log s}{\sqrt{s}})$，随时间趋于零。

结论: 所提出的KL正则化随机化框架能有效近似经典最优切换控制问题，镜像下降流在退火温度调度下可实现收敛至经典最优值函数。

局限 / 后续问题: 

中文摘要: 我们研究连续时间强化学习中的最优切换问题，其中决策者通过在有限多个状态之间切换来控制扩散过程，同时产生运行成本和切换成本。为了实现探索，我们将经典的确定性切换控制松弛为随机化框架，其中切换决策由具有状态依赖生成元的连续时间马尔可夫链控制，并在成本泛函中增加以温度参数 $λ$ 为权重的KL散度正则化项。在系数的温和假设下，我们证明正则化值函数是椭圆型Hamilton--Jacobi--Bellman系统的唯一光滑解，并推导出由值函数在各个模式间差值的指数变换给出的显式最优Gibbs策略。我们进一步证明正则化值函数以 $O\left(λ\log \frac{1}{λ}\right)$ 阶误差逼近经典最优值函数，这与其它熵正则化控制问题中建立的类似界一致，且被认为是紧的。为了数值求解正则化问题，我们在对偶对数策略空间中引入镜像下降流，证明其适定性以及值函数沿流的单调递减性，并建立到经典最优值函数的定量误差界。对于恒定温度调度，收敛速率为 $O\left(\frac{1}{e^{λs} - 1}+λ\log\frac{1}{λ}\right)$ 阶；而在退火调度 $λ_s = \frac{1}{\sqrt{1+s}}$ 下，我们得到 $O\left(\frac{\log s}{\sqrt{s}}\right)$ 阶的速率，该速率随流时间 $s \to \infty$ 趋于零。

英文原始摘要: We study continuous-time reinforcement learning for the optimal switching problem, in which a decision-maker controls a diffusion process by switching among finitely many regimes, incurring both running and transition costs. To enable exploration, we relax the classical deterministic switching control to a randomized framework, where the switching decisions are governed by a continuous-time Markov chain with state-dependent generator, and augment the cost functional with a KL-divergence regularization weighted by a temperature parameter $λ$. Under mild assumptions on the coefficients, we establish that the regularized value function is the unique smooth solution of an elliptic Hamilton--Jacobi--Bellman system, and derive an explicit optimal Gibbs policy given by an exponential transformation of the value function differences across modes. We further prove that the regularized value function approximates the classical optimal value function with error of order $O\left(λ\log \frac{1}λ\right)$, which is consistent with analogous bounds established in other entropy-regularized control problems and is believed to be sharp. To solve the regularized problem numerically, we introduce a mirror descent flow in the dual logarithmic policy space, prove its well-posedness and the monotonic decrease of the value function along the flow, and establish quantitative error bound to the classical optimal value function. For a constant temperature scheduler, the convergence rate is of order $O\left(\frac{1}{e^{λs} - 1}+λ\log\frac1λ\right)$, while under the annealing scheduler $λ_s = \frac{1}{\sqrt{1+s}}$, we obtain the rate $O\left(\frac{\log s}{\sqrt{s}}\right)$, which decays to zero as the flow time $s \to \infty$.

</details>

英文原始摘要: The transition to electric heavy-duty freight is constrained by a strong interdependence between vehicle adoption and charging infrastructure deployment. While system dynamics models are well-suited to simulate these socio-technical feedback loops, their reliance on conditional logic and heuristic rules makes the underlying dynamics difficult to interpret mathematically. This limits the direct application of formal systems and control theory. This paper proposes a solution to that problem through a general hybrid system identification framework that extracts a continuous-time analytical surrogate from simulations of complex system dynamics. The approach combines the sparse identification of nonlinear dynamics algorithm with neural ordinary differential equations to form a grey-box model. The first component identifies the dominant interpretable dynamics under causal coupling constraints, while the neural residual captures unmodelled nonlinearities. The framework is trained using multiple shooting over a 40-year horizon. The resulting model reproduces the training trajectories with a normalized root-mean-square error below 4\%, while maintaining reliable predictive accuracy when evaluated on unseen initial conditions.

英文原始摘要: Tempered time-fractional coupled phase-field (tTFCP) systems are used to model interfacial phenomena involving memory-dependent transport and relaxation mechanisms. Numerical solutions to these systems are challenging due to the simultaneous presence of nonlocal temporal operators, weak initial singularities, moving diffuse interfaces, and strongly coupled multiphysics dynamics. In this work, we introduce FM-tfPINN (fractional-memory physics-informed neural network), which is used for forward simulation and inverse parameter identification in tempered fractional coupled phase-field systems. Unlike conventional fractional PINNs, which enforce memory effects solely through residual constraints, our framework incorporates tempered fractional memory directly into the neural representation via latent memory-source functions and a tempered fractional integral operator. We develop a fast shifted residual formulation based on graded temporal meshes and sum-of-exponentials (SOE) history compression to efficiently evaluate the tempered fractional operators. This framework combines interface-aware and residual-adaptive collocation strategies, improving resolution near evolving diffuse interfaces. A unified, physics-informed loss formulation allows for the forward prediction and inverse recovery of unknown physical parameters from sparse observations.
  We assess the proposed method on a class of tempered fractional corrosion phase-field models, including one-dimensional corrosion-front propagation, activation- and diffusion-controlled regimes, two-dimensional pitting corrosion, and inverse mobility identification problems. The numerical results demonstrate the accurate recovery of coupled phase and concentration fields, the robust prediction of physically relevant interface diagnostics, and the reliable estimation of parameters from limited data.

### [133] [Multi-type branching inference on contact trees with application to COVID-19](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19405v2)
*Augustine Okolie,Johannes Müller,Eno Akarawakc,Isaac Ajiboye*

一句话结论: 提出基于接触树的多类型分支似然框架，结合接触度异质性推断传播动态与接触结构。

研究问题: 现有基于树的似然方法大多假设均匀混合，无法捕捉个体在感染更多接触者后传播潜力的变化，缺乏从传播树中推断传播动态与接触结构的有效框架。

主要创新点: 提出直接在传播树上操作的似然框架，不依赖序列数据，将每个感染个体用有效接触者总数和已感染下游接触者数表征，推导出闭式常微分方程，并将接触度异质性纳入多类型分支似然中。


<details>
  <summary>更多信息</summary>

研究动机: 传染病动态理解需要从传播树中推断流行病学参数，但现有方法忽略接触度异质性，无法反映个体传播潜力随感染接触者增加而变化的现实。

主要方法: 在根接触树上建立随机SIR过程的似然函数，推导子支完全未被观测的概率和产生观测叶节点概率密度的闭式常微分方程；对部分解析的树将内部分支时间作为潜变量处理。

实验 / 验证: 在模拟暴发数据上验证参数恢复和不确定性校准，并应用于印度卡纳塔克邦的COVID-19接触追踪实证数据。

主要结果: 模拟实验显示参数恢复准确且不确定性校准良好；实证数据应用展示了框架在真实流行病学场景中的实用性。

结论: 该框架为从完全或部分解析的传播树推断传播动态和接触结构提供了有原则的基线，补充而非依赖基于序列的系统发育动力学推断。

局限 / 后续问题: 

中文摘要: 从传播树中推断流行病学参数对于理解传染病动态至关重要。现有的基于树的似然方法，包括最初应用于系统发育动力学设置的多类型生灭模型，提供了强大的工具，但大多数假设均匀混合，很少捕捉传播潜力如何随着个体感染更多接触者而变化。在本研究中，我们开发了一个直接在传播树上操作的似然框架，其中节点是个体，边是报告的传播事件，不涉及序列数据。我们推导了根接触树上随机SIR过程的似然函数，其中每个感染个体由有效接触者总数和已感染的下游接触者数量来表征。我们获得了子支完全未被观测到的概率以及其在给定状态下产生观测（采样）叶节点的概率密度的闭式常微分方程。所得似然函数可在已知叶节点状态的根接触树上进行评估，我们通过将内部分支时间视为潜变量将其扩展到部分解析的树。对模拟暴发的验证证实了准确的参数恢复和良好校准的不确定性。对印度卡纳塔克邦的COVID-19接触追踪数据的应用展示了该框架在真实流行病学环境中的实用性。通过在多类型分支似然中纳入接触度异质性，我们的工作为从完全或部分解析的传播树中推断传播动态和接触结构提供了有原则的基线，补充而非依赖于基于序列的系统发育动力学推断。

英文原始摘要: Inferring epidemiological parameters from transmission trees is essential for understanding infectious disease dynamics. Existing tree-based likelihood methods, including the multi-type birth-death models originally applied in phylodynamic settings, provide powerful tools, but most assume homogeneous mixing and rarely capture how transmission potential changes as an individual infects more of their contacts. In this work, we develop a likelihood framework that operates directly on transmission trees, in which nodes are individuals and edges are reported transmission events, with no sequence data involved. We derive a likelihood for a stochastic SIR process on a rooted contact tree in which each infected individual is characterised by the total number of effective contacts, and the number of already infected downstream contacts. We obtain closed-form ordinary differential equations for the probability that a clade goes entirely unobserved and for the probability density that it produces an observed (sampled) tip in a given state. The resulting likelihood can be evaluated for a rooted contact tree with known tip states, and we extend it to partially resolved trees by treating internal branching times as latent variables. Validation on simulated outbreaks confirms accurate parameter recovery and well calibrated uncertainty. Application to empirical COVID-19 contact-tracing data from Karnataka, India, demonstrates the framework's utility for real epidemiological settings. By incorporating contact-degree heterogeneity in a multi-type branching likelihood, our work provides a principled baseline for inferring both transmission dynamics and contact structure from fully or partially resolved transmission trees, complementing rather than relying on sequence-based phylodynamic inference

### [134] [Counting and Sampling Anti-Ferromagnetic Potts Models on Random Regular Bipartite Graphs in the Non-uniqueness Regime](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21250v1)
*Zhidan Li,Siyu Liu,Kuan Yang*

一句话结论: 在随机正则二部图上证明了低温Potts模型Glauber动力学混合缓慢，并给出确定性配分函数逼近算法。

研究问题: 在随机正则二部图（高概率为良好扩展图）上，低温反铁磁多态Potts模型配分函数的逼近问题，包括Glauber动力学的混合时间分析和确定性逼近算法的设计。

主要创新点: 将反铁磁Ising模型的缓慢混合结果推广至多态Potts模型，同时基于抽象聚合物模型框架设计了确定性配分函数逼近算法，在扩展图上同时给出负面与正面结果。

  <summary>更多信息</summary>

研究动机: 反铁磁Potts模型的相变与计算复杂性理论及配分函数逼近密切相关；在格点上已有相变与缓慢混合的结果，但在随机正则二部图（扩展图）上的低温行为尚待研究。

主要方法: 负面方面：推广Geisler等人的Ising模型方法，证明温度相对于度数充分低时单点Glauber动力学混合时间指数级缓慢。正面方面：采用抽象聚合物模型框架，借鉴Jenssen等人、Liao等人的方法设计确定性逼近算法。

实验 / 验证: 本文为理论工作，无数值实验；通过数学证明建立混合时间下界和算法逼近保证。

主要结果: 证明了当温度相对于图度数充分低时，Glauber动力学混合时间为指数级缓慢；同时给出了基于抽象聚合物模型的确定性算法，能够逼近配分函数。

结论: 在随机正则二部图上，低温反铁磁多态Potts模型既存在Glauber动力学的计算困难性（指数缓慢混合），也存在确定性多项式逼近算法的可行性，两者通过温度与度数的关系界定。

局限 / 后续问题: 结果限于随机正则二部图且要求温度相对于度数充分低；对一般图或更宽温度范围的情形尚未涉及。

中文摘要: 反铁磁多态Potts模型是Ising模型的推广，是统计物理学中最基本的模型之一。Kotecký（Phys. Rev. B, 1985）猜想该模型在格点上经历从无穷高温下的无序相到充分低温下的有序相的相变。此类相变被认为在计算复杂性理论中起重要作用，并与系统配分函数的逼近问题密切相关。对于正常三着色模型（对应零温度情形），Galvin、Kahn、Randall和Sorkin（SIDMA, 2015）证明了格上一族局部更新马尔可夫链的缓慢混合，这与Feldheim和Spinka（J. Eur. Math. Soc., 2019）所证明的相共存现象一致。在本工作中，我们研究在随机正则二部图（以高概率为良好的二部扩展图）上低温反铁磁多态Potts模型配分函数的逼近问题。在负面结果方面，我们将Geisler、Kang、Sarantis和Wdowinski（arXiv, 2026）关于反铁磁Ising模型的结果推广到多态Potts模型，证明当温度相对于底层图的度数充分低时，著名的单点Glauber动力学具有指数级缓慢的混合时间。在正面结果方面，我们设计了一种确定性算法，通过抽象聚合物模型框架对模型的配分函数进行逼近，该框架沿用了Jenssen、Keevash和Perkins（SICOMP, 2020），Liao、Lin、Lu和Mao（Theor. Comput. Sci., 2022），Galanis、Goldberg和Stewart（TOCT, 2021）以及Geisler、Kang、Sarantis和Wdowinski（arXiv, 2026）的工作。

英文原始摘要: The anti-ferromagnetic multi-state Potts model, a generalization of the Ising model, is one of the most fundamental models in statistical physics. It was conjectured by Kotecký (Phys.~Rev.~B, 1985) that the model undergoes a phase transition from a disordered phase at infinite temperature to an ordered phase at sufficiently low temperature on lattices. Such phase transitions are believed to play an important role in computational complexity theory and remain closely connected to the problem of approximating the partition function of the system. For proper three-coloring models (corresponding to the zero-temperature), torpid mixing of a family of local-update Markov chains on lattices was established by Galvin, Kahn, Randall and Sorkin (SIDMA, 2015), coinciding with the presence of phase coexistence following shown by Feldheim and Spinka (J.~Eur.~Math.~Soc., 2019).
  In this work, we study approximating the partition function of the anti-ferromagnetic multi-state Potts model at low temperature on random regular bipartite graphs, which are with high probability good bipartite expanders. On the negative side, we generalize the result by Geisler, Kang, Sarantis and Wdowinski (arXiv, 2026) for anti-ferromagnetic Ising models to show that when the temperature is sufficiently low relative to the degree of the underlying graph, the celebrated single-site Glauber dynamics has exponentially slow mixing time. On the positive side, we design a deterministic algorithm that yields an approximation to the partition function of the model via the framework of abstract polymer models as Jenssen, Keevash and Perkins (SICOMP, 2020), Liao, Lin, Lu and Mao (Theor.~Comput.~Sci., 2022), Galanis, Goldberg and Stewart (TOCT, 2021) and Geisler, Kang, Sarantis and Wdowinski (arXiv, 2026).

### [135] [TopoCast: A Topological Fidelity Framework for Evaluating Transformer-Based Time Series Forecasting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.25439v1)

主要创新点: 提出TopoCast框架，结合Takens延迟嵌入与持续同调从拓扑角度评估预测的结构保真度，推导出拓扑保真度分数（TFS）；并引入主导周期重叠指标，构建局部拓扑保真度分数（LTFS），捕获相位感知的时间定位误差。


<details>
  <summary>更多信息</summary>

研究动机: 传统逐点误差指标无法反映预测信号的结构特性，使得结构退化的预测仍能获得良好评分，亟需能够评估结构保真度的新方法。

主要方法: 利用Takens延迟嵌入重构预测与真实序列的相空间表示，应用持续同调表征内在动态，从持续图推导四个互补的拓扑保真度度量并聚合为TFS；进一步引入主导周期重叠指标将拓扑特征映射到时间域，结合TFS形成LTFS。

实验 / 验证: 在三个真实世界基准数据集上对五种Transformer架构进行实验评估。

主要结果: 具有相似预测误差的模型表现出截然不同的结构保真度特征，揭示了传统评估所忽略的失败模式。

结论: 拓扑感知的预测评估能够发现传统误差指标无法捕捉的结构退化问题，为时间序列预测评估提供了新的视角和工具。

局限 / 后续问题: 

中文摘要: 基于深度学习的模型在时间序列预测（TSF）中取得了最先进的性能，然而其评估仍然被逐点误差指标（如均方误差MSE）所主导，这些指标量化了数值精度却忽略了预测信号的结构特性，包括递归动态、振荡行为和相位对齐。因此，表现出过度平滑、相位偏移或频率失真的预测可能在存在显著结构退化的情况下仍获得良好的误差分数。为解决这一局限性，我们提出了TopoCast，一个用于评估TSF结构保真度的拓扑驱动框架。TopoCast利用Takens延迟嵌入重构预测序列和真实序列的相空间表示，并应用持续同调来表征其内在动态特性。我们从持续图中推导出四个互补的拓扑保真度度量，并将其聚合为拓扑保真度分数（TFS）。我们进一步引入了主导周期重叠，一种将持久拓扑特征映射到时间域以评估主导振荡模式是否出现在正确时间点的新颖指标。结合TFS，这产生了局部拓扑保真度分数（LTFS），一种相位感知度量，能够捕获现有评估指标无法察觉的时间定位误差。在三个真实世界基准数据集上对五种Transformer架构的实验表明，具有相似预测误差的模型可以表现出截然不同的结构保真度特征，揭示了传统评估所忽略的失败模式，并突出了拓扑感知预测评估的价值。

英文原始摘要: Deep learning-based models have achieved state-of-the-art performance in Time Series Forecasting (TSF), yet their evaluation remains dominated by pointwise error metrics such as Mean Squared Error (MSE), which quantify numerical accuracy but overlook structural properties of the forecast signal, including recurrent dynamics, oscillatory behavior, and phase alignment. As a result, forecasts exhibiting over-smoothing, phase shifts, or frequency distortions may achieve favorable error scores despite substantial structural degradation. To address this limitation, we propose TopoCast, a topology-driven framework for evaluating structural fidelity in TSF. TopoCast reconstructs phase-space representations of forecast and ground-truth sequences using Takens delay embedding and applies persistent homology to characterize their intrinsic dynamics. We derive four complementary topological fidelity measures from persistence diagrams and aggregate them into a Topological Fidelity Score (TFS). We further introduce dominant cycle overlap, a novel metric that maps persistent topological features to the temporal domain to assess whether dominant oscillatory patterns occur at the correct time points. Combined with TFS, this yields the Localized Topological Fidelity Score (LTFS), a phase-aware measure that captures temporal localization errors invisible to existing evaluation metrics. Experiments on five Transformer architectures across three real-world benchmark datasets demonstrate that models with similar forecasting errors can exhibit markedly different structural fidelity profiles, revealing failure modes overlooked by conventional evaluation and highlighting the value of topology-aware forecast assessment.

英文原始摘要: Multivariate time series anomaly detection (MTSAD) is critical for a wide range of application areas, such as industrial monitoring, cybersecurity, or healthcare. Real-world data is often sparse, irregularly sampled or partially observed, yet existing methods assume uniformly sampled time series. We propose a generative approach based on Latent SDEs that projects the observed time series on a continuous-time stochastic dynamical system, directly being able to handle missing observations and irregular sampling, while also naturally capturing possible cyclic behavior that many real-world use cases inherently possess. Experiments on six anomaly benchmark datasets show that our proposed method ranks first among state-of-the-art baselines. We further demonstrate that our method remains robust under severe data sparsity, while performance significantly degrades for the tested baseline methods. These results highlight latent SDEs as a natural inductive bias for anomaly detection in multivariate time series, especially in presence of real-world irregularities.

  <summary>更多信息</summary>

研究动机: 母机制（引力波冻入）产生无质量暗费米子但无法自洽地提供质量，需要一种几何框架来消除对额外质量参数的依赖，从而将遗迹丰度简化为单一标度的函数。

主要方法: 发展QSL的Einstein-Cartan推广，构造单一狄拉克场的旋量1-形式并验证其纯自旋1/2性质，通过显式Clifford约化分析宇宙学旋量凝聚体源出的矢量迹挠曲对费米子质量项的贡献。

实验 / 验证: 本文为理论工作，无物理实验；通过解析推导计算有效质量与哈勃率的关系及遗迹丰度对标度H_*的依赖。

主要结果: 挠曲赋予费米子纯狄拉克质量M_eff=(1/√6)|dotχ/χ|≃(c_χ/√6)H_*，无赝标量或交叉项；遗迹丰度Ωh²∝H_*^{5/2}，仅依赖单一标度；论文II确认自旋1/2狄拉克费米子为唯一QSL暗物质候选者。

结论: QSL框架以几何方式提供了引力波冻入机制所需的质量，消除了自由参数，使暗物质遗迹丰度由单一标度H_*决定；复合自旋1/2狄拉克费米子是唯一的暗物质候选者。

局限 / 后续问题: 摘要未明确提及实验或观测验证途径；暗物质唯象学与渐近自由标量场宇宙学的具体联系有待进一步探讨。

中文摘要: Maleknejad和Kopp（2026）提出的引力波诱导冻入机制通过随机引力波背景产生暗费米子，但需要通过其他途径使这些费米子获得质量。我们发展了广义相对论的二次旋量拉格朗日（QSL）表述，并将其推广至Einstein-Cartan理论，作为一个以几何方式提供该质量的框架。由单一狄拉克场构建的旋量1-形式是纯自旋1/2的——其gamma无迹（自旋3/2）部分恒为零——因此传播激发为狄拉克费米子，与所产生的外尔费米子具有相同内容。宇宙学旋量凝聚体源出一个矢量迹挠曲K∝dotχ/χ，显式Clifford约化表明该挠曲赋予费米子纯狄拉克质量M_eff=(1/√6)|dotχ/χ|，不含赝标量或交叉项。该质量不是自由参数，而是锁定到产生时的哈勃率M_eff≃(c_χ/√6)H_*，使遗迹丰度本质上是单一标度H_*的函数（Ωh²∝H_*^{5/2}），并提供了母机制必须假设的质量。将旋量1-形式提升为独立场是否产生传播的自旋3/2候选者是一个独立的动力学问题；论文II表明并非如此——QSL将所有传播通道归入引力扇区——因此复合自旋1/2狄拉克费米子是唯一的QSL暗物质候选者。我们讨论了由此产生的暗物质唯象学及其与渐近自由标量场宇宙学的联系。

英文原始摘要: The gravitational-wave induced freeze-in of Maleknejad and Kopp (2026) produces dark fermions from a stochastic gravitational-wave background, but requires them to acquire mass by separate means. We develop the Quadratic Spinor Lagrangian (QSL) formulation of general relativity, extended to Einstein--Cartan, as a framework that supplies this mass geometrically. The spinor 1-form built from a single Dirac field is purely spin-1/2 -- its gamma-traceless (spin-3/2) part vanishes identically -- so the propagating excitation is a Dirac fermion, the same content as the produced Weyl fermion. A cosmological spinor condensate sources a vectorial trace torsion $K\propto\dotχ/χ$, and an explicit Clifford reduction shows that this torsion gives the fermion a pure Dirac mass $M_{eff}=(1/\sqrt6)\,|\dotχ/χ|$, with no pseudoscalar or cross terms. The mass is not a free parameter but is locked to the Hubble rate at production, $M_{eff}\simeq(c_χ/\sqrt6)H_*$, making the relic abundance a function of essentially the single scale $H_*$ ($Ωh^2\propto H_*^{5/2}$) and supplying the mass the parent mechanism must postulate. Whether promoting the spinor 1-form to an independent field yields a propagating spin-3/2 candidate is a distinct dynamical question; Paper II shows that it does not -- the QSL channels all propagation into the gravitational sector -- so the composite spin-1/2 Dirac fermion is the unique QSL dark-matter candidate. We discuss the resulting dark-matter phenomenology and its link to asymptotically free scalar-field cosmology.
